League of Nations Administrative Council Meeting; Japan Worries About Discussion of Non-Recognition of Puppet State; Hirota Cables Ito to Rush to Geneva

China Cooperates with the League of Nations on Opium Prohibition

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council held a closed meeting at 10:40 a.m. this morning to discuss administrative and budgetary issues. Dr. Wellington Koo represented China and attended. The public meeting began half an hour late to discuss issues such as knowledge cooperation, the establishment of the International Committee on Intellectual Cooperation, and the report of the Opium Committee. The Japanese representative did not attend, but several secretaries were present to listen. The public meeting lasted for three quarters of an hour. Dr. Koo endorsed the Opium Report, saying that China is determined to earnestly deal with the opium problem and the trade in dangerous narcotics. Dr. Koo proposed that methods be formulated quickly so that the government can comply with conventions to restrict the sale and manufacture of narcotics. The public meeting of the Administrative Council was then adjourned until 10:30 a.m. tomorrow morning. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd) (Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council meeting began secretly this morning, deciding to postpone discussion of the Assyrian massacre case at the request of the Iraqi government, and then officially opened at 11:40 a.m. With this important and difficult issue postponed, it passed several reports today on issues such as opium prohibition, international intellectual cooperation, and the establishment of the International Building Committee. Chinese representative Wellington Koo stated that China will soon join the 1931 Convention on Limiting the Manufacture and Distribution of Dangerous Drugs. The Assyrian issue is expected to be one of the most difficult issues that must be handled at this session because France accuses the Iraqi government of mistreating the Assyrians, forcing them to flee the country. So far, France and Iraq are still in dispute. It is expected that France will ask the League of Nations to pay attention to Iraq's declaration to the League of Nations on May 30, 1932, guaranteeing full protection of all ethnic groups within the country without discrimination on the basis of language, race, or religion. However, the Iraqi representative here claimed that the Iraqi government has been studying methods for implementing the League of Nations resolution on the Assyrians within the country since November of last year. The dispute between France and Iraq this time was caused by the fact that the Assyrians in Syria were not completely disarmed and could attack Iraqi sentries. (Guomin dispatch, 22nd)

(Tokyo) The League of Nations Council is scheduled to meet in Geneva on the 22nd. This meeting will discuss the report of the advisory committee established by the resolution of non-recognition of (Manchukuo) and the speech of the Chinese representative. Foreign Minister Hirota attaches importance to this matter and yesterday cabled Ito Shuji, Director of the League of Nations Imperial Affairs Bureau, and Counselor Yokoyama to rush to Geneva. (Dentsu dispatch, 22nd)

(Tokyo) Although Japan has withdrawn from the League of Nations, it will always cooperate with cultural facilities for the betterment of mankind. This is the policy of the Japanese government and has been stated repeatedly. The term of Dr. Aikitsu Tanakadate, a member of the Committee on Intellectual Cooperation, which is suitable for the League of Nations Council meeting starting on the 22nd, is about to expire and will be re-elected. The Foreign Ministry intends to recommend Dr. Inazo Nitobe as his successor. After Dr. Nitobe returns from the Banff Pacific Conference, he will be consulted. In order to dispel misunderstandings about the Japanese government after withdrawing from the League of Nations, the Foreign Ministry believes that Dr. Nitobe, a scholar with international credibility, is the most suitable candidate, so it has decided to recommend him. (Dentsu dispatch, 22nd)

(Geneva) Amidst the most serious European political atmosphere since the end of the European War, the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting will open tomorrow. The first meeting will be a closed meeting as usual to discuss important internal administrative issues of the Council. The public meeting will be held in the afternoon to handle routine matters. The terms of Ireland and Norway as members of the current session have expired. According to the situation today, it is expected that the League of Nations General Assembly will elect Australia and Denmark to succeed them. All the more important proposals at this Administrative Council meeting will probably be discussed starting next week. Current difficult issues include the political tension between Germany and Austria. Because Britain, Italy, and other countries are very anxious about the frequent incidents on the German-Austrian border, the League of Nations will have to discuss them. Another example is the issue of Germany's treatment of Jews. It is heard that the petitions and supporting documents sent by international conferences from various places received by the League of Nations Secretariat are almost a foot high, and it will be impossible not to have a public debate on them. Furthermore, according to the situation in the lounge today, there is currently an attempt to publicly debate the current turbulent political situation in the world. League of Nations leaders believe that it is their responsibility to dispel the turbulence in the world. These issues are better handled by the League of Nations than by diplomatic talks between countries. In addition, the dispute between France and the Kingdom of Iraq over the issue of Syrian refugees also seems likely to be brought to the Administrative Council meeting. (Guomin dispatch, 21st) (Geneva) The French government sent a memorandum to the League of Nations regarding the massacre of Assyrian Christian minorities in Iraq, asking it to be distributed to all member states. The League of Nations Secretariat today specifically announced this memorandum. According to the circumstances, after the massacre of Assyrian Christians in Iraq in early August of this year, the Iraqi government involved the French government, which was mandated to govern Syria. The French government therefore presented this memorandum to clarify. The contents of the French memorandum detail the border situation, which is essential to understanding the incident, and then analyzes and explains the incident, saying (On the Syrian side, officials responsible for maintaining border order have always maintained an extremely fair attitude towards the Iraqi government. Regarding incidents occurring on the border and difficulties caused by the large number of Assyrian Christians fleeing to Syria, Syrian French officials, regardless of the size of the matter, must report to the Iraqi government on a daily basis. When the leaders of the Assyrian Christians requested entry into the Syrian border, French officials ordered them to hand over the weapons they were carrying for safekeeping, and they could not be used within the territory of Syria during their stay. At the end of July of this year, Assyrian Christians, knowing that Syria was difficult to accommodate, contacted the Iraqi authorities again to surrender. The Assyrians then informed the Syrian French officials that they had reached an agreement and were willing to return to Iraq and requested the return of their original weapons. The French authorities granted their request and returned the weapons. The Assyrians then crossed the Tigris River to the east, and gunfire broke out. At that time, Iraqi troops were setting up machine guns on the river and firing head-on. On August 8, several people transported the wounded back to the west bank of the river, and Iraqi aircraft followed and bombed them. (Havas dispatch, 21st)

British Representatives Exert Themselves to Clear the Thorns of Disarmament

Continuing Consultations with France, Italy, Germany, and the United States

(London) This afternoon, British Ambassador Sir Eric Phipps will host a banquet at his embassy to entertain British Foreign Secretary Sir John Simon, Undersecretary Anthony Eden, Lord President of the Council Baldwin, French Premier Daladier, and Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour. Sir John Simon and Anthony Eden will fly from London to here this morning, and Baldwin has already arrived here. After the banquet, Britain and France will continue to discuss the draft disarmament treaty. Then, Sir John Simon and Anthony Eden will go to Geneva to attend the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting and the League of Nations General Assembly. Daladier will probably go to Geneva on Sunday and will talk with Baldwin at the end of the week if necessary. The British representatives will consult with the representatives of France, Italy, Germany, and the United States in Geneva, hoping to clear the thorns hindering progress and make the British draft accepted by the public, so that the Disarmament Conference can be resumed in October. What is currently exciting is that the feelings between France and Italy are gradually getting closer. This is particularly relevant because the power of Italian Premier Mussolini can extend to the German government. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd)

Roosevelt Considers Controlling Monetary Policy

To Make the Price of the Dollar Tend Toward Stability; The Government Purchases Agricultural Products to Relief the Poor

(Washington) It is heard that the authorities are currently seriously considering a plan to give the managed dollar a strong purchasing power so that prices can be fixed. The President has the power to determine the gold content of the dollar for any specified period, which can be specified monthly or quarterly. (Reuters dispatch, 21st)

(New York) President Roosevelt's intention to implement a "managed currency" policy, seeking to keep the purchasing power of the dollar unchanged for a long time, is now becoming increasingly clear. Financial figures say that although the government has expressed opposition to a true monetary inflation policy, it is actually implementing a lending inflation policy, such as the Federal Reserve Bank purchasing government bonds and releasing loans through the Financial Rehabilitation Corporation. In addition, the government is spending huge sums of money on agriculture and public works. The government is now studying a large-scale plan to recirculate the 60 billion yuan of funds stagnating in the closed or liquidating banks. The government also intends to purchase half of the cotton harvest at a price of 15 cents per pound to satisfy cotton farmers (the current value of cotton is 10 cents per pound), provided that various cotton farmers agree to reduce the amount of the next harvest according to this number. If this plan is effective, other growers will also demand the same treatment from the government. (Havas dispatch, 21st) (Washington) Roosevelt wants to find ways to eliminate surplus agricultural products to raise prices and is studying new methods to relieve unemployment. He recently ordered the Department of Agriculture to adjust agriculture and ordered the Federal Agricultural Relief Bureau to purchase 75 million worth of beef, milk, and poultry to distribute to the poor. He also plans to purchase cotton to make clothes and provide relief to the poor. Various states and the federal government have already carried out relief efforts. In the past, 100,000 hogs were purchased from hog farmers and have begun to be distributed to the poor. The current purchase is for another batch. There are now 3.5 million people who have registered and are waiting for relief. (Havas dispatch, 21st)

Pro-Inflation and Anti-Inflation Factions Clearly Defined

(Washington) All the newspapers in the United States today are fighting against the pro-inflation members of Congress, while senators who do not support inflation have also gathered under Roosevelt's banner. Roosevelt knows that the pro-inflation faction in Congress will openly break with the government in January next year, but he is determined to follow the original policy, stating clearly that reducing the value of gold yuan, printing more greenbacks, and other inflation schemes are not currently in the government's plan. Senator Lewis was the first to assist the government in the battle, declaring that inflation would destroy the industrial recovery plan. However, the power of the pro-inflation faction is also very strong. The government itself has investigated the attitude of members of Congress. Those who support inflation currently constitute a majority in both houses. Only after prices, especially cotton prices, have increased significantly can the attitude of the members of Congress be changed. The southern states account for the vast majority of power in the Democratic government, and now, due to the extraordinary drop in cotton prices in the past four years, most have become pro-inflation. (Guomin She dispatch, 21st)

Cairo, Guomin News, 21st: The Egyptian cabinet resigned today. The reason is not yet fully understood. After Egyptian Prime Minister Sidqi reorganized the cabinet in January, he suffered a serious illness. Although he went to Europe for recuperation, his physical condition did not recover. He originally intended to resign alone a few days ago. After a doctor's diagnosis, his health was considered to be good, so he decided not to resign temporarily on the 8th of this month. Therefore, the sudden resignation of the entire cabinet was completely unexpected.

Reichstag Fire Trial Begins; Main Defendant Feigns Madness in Court

Reuters, Leipzig, 21st: The Dutch defendant in the Reichstag fire trial, Lubbe, appeared in court today dressed in coarse cloth, with his hands tied behind his back and iron chains around his waist, to be interrogated. At the start of the trial, the presiding judge ordered his handcuffs to be removed. Evidence was presented to show that Lubbe had been mentally abnormal since childhood and had a tendency to commit crimes. It was also shown that he had attempted to join the National Socialist Party, whose aim was to overthrow the German constitution by force. The arson was merely a minor aspect of their crimes.

Reuters, Leipzig, 22nd: At the start of the Reichstag fire trial yesterday, the defendant Lubbe exhibited signs of madness during questioning. A psychiatrist was summoned to examine his mental state. The psychiatrist stated that Lubbe's nerves were normal, but he could not determine whether his behavior was natural or feigned. The presiding judge stated that Lubbe's mad laughter yesterday suggested a mental illness. The psychiatrist then stated that Lubbe had gone on a hunger strike in prison to expedite the trial, and then resumed eating. During today's hearing, the police chief of Breslau stated that a "Brown Book" published on September 1, which contained accusations of National Socialist atrocities and claimed that the Reichstag fire was ordered by Hitler's propaganda minister Goebbels and that the plan was poorly executed, was entirely fabricated. The prosecutor then read a news item from a Dutch newspaper stating that prison officials had withheld a letter from Lubbe's family regarding his defense. As a result, Lubbe's family had petitioned President Hindenburg for assistance. The presiding judge asked Lubbe about the letter. Lubbe insisted that he had not received it and that it must be in prison. The court then adjourned to allow Lubbe to meet with Dutch lawyer Dr. Storm Pol, who had been hired by Lubbe's family and had flown to Leipzig to defend Lubbe.

Mutiny of the Guard of the Xinjiang Governor's Office Unsuccessful

Sheng Shicai Telegraphed Beijing to Report

(Nanjing) The guard of the Xinjiang Governor's Office, incited by others, plotted a mutiny, but it was discovered and stopped before it could cause any trouble. Sheng Shicai telegraphed a report to Beijing, the original text of which is as follows:

Respectfully presented to Chairman Lin of the Central Executive Committee of the National Government, Premier Wang of the Executive Yuan, the Military Affairs Commission, the General Staff Headquarters, the Ministry of Military Affairs, and Chairman Chiang in Guling: Previously, Ma Zhongying repeatedly sent his representatives Zhang Yashao and Yao Zhiping to the province to discuss seeking peace due to defeat. I, Shicai, followed the benevolent intentions of the Central Government and stopped the victorious army, refraining from pursuing the defeated enemy. I also sent the Chief of Staff of the Governor's Office, Liu Bin, to negotiate the peace. It was agreed that Ma's army would withdraw from Turpan and concentrate in Hami, and that I would appoint Ma as the East Route Garrison Commander. Politics would be subject to the Chairman, and military affairs would be subject to the Governor. Ma signed and agreed to each item. The details have been telegraphed and reported previously. However, for almost two months, Ma's army has been stationed in Turpan without any intention of withdrawing. On the 9th of this month, Minister Luo went to Turpan for inspection. Chairman Liu sent the Administrative Director, Li Rong, and I sent the Chief of Staff, Liu Bin, and my younger brother, Shiqi, to accompany him as hostages, intending to show our sincerity and invite Ma to the province for detailed discussions to seek long-term peace and stability. Unexpectedly, Ma Zhongying was suspicious and did not advance, but instead invited me and Chairman Liu to meet in Daban City. Considering that Ma Zhongying had already assumed the military position I had appointed him to, such a request was arrogant in terms of status and rank. However, in order to resolve the situation and alleviate the Central Government's concerns in the west, I and Chairman Liu decided to humble ourselves and meet him on the 16th. Unexpectedly, Yao Zhiping and others instigated a mutiny of the Governor's Office guard between the two parties. Fortunately, the officers and soldiers of the guard were not entirely deceived and reported it, so it was prevented in advance and did not cause any trouble. It is difficult to guess whether Ma instructed Yao and others to take such absurd actions. To prevent any future problems, I had to temporarily put Yao and others under surveillance. After careful consideration, I, Shicai, could not bear to lightly start a war and cause suffering to the people again. I still hope that Ma Zhongying will deeply realize the danger of the overall situation and the plight of the people's livelihoods. I have sent a letter by special envoy, asking him to send another representative to the province to continue negotiations. As long as there is a glimmer of hope for peace, I, Shicai, will do everything possible to achieve it. Further developments will be telegraphed and reported. I humbly request your review and approval. The Xinjiang Border Defense Governor, Sheng Shicai, kowtows. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Dutch Authorities in Indonesia Ban Firecrackers, Interfering with Religious Etiquette; Overseas Chinese Protest

Following the example of the authorities in the Straits Settlements, the Dutch East Indies government is now engaged in banning the setting off of firecrackers within its jurisdiction. Overseas Chinese in Batavia and Surabaya have lodged a strong protest, stating that the government has no right to interfere with the religious etiquette of residents and that if the government insists on banning them, it should purchase the firecrackers stored by merchants and compensate them for the losses, or allocate funds to transport the firecrackers back to China. (Reuters, 22nd)

Chen Jiongming Dies of Illness

(Hong Kong) Chen Jiongming died of illness at his residence in Hong Kong on the evening of the 21st. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Hong Kong) After his defeat, Chen Jiongming secretly went to Pingjin, Qingdao, and Siam, hoping to stage a comeback, but all attempts were unsuccessful. In recent years, he lived in seclusion in Hong Kong, quite depressed. Most of the industries he operated went bankrupt, so he often appeared embarrassed. His lifelong friends Lin Yishun and others also gradually drifted apart. In August of this year, he suddenly suffered from enteritis and was admitted to the Matilda Hospital for treatment. Although the fever subsided after half a month, the doctor advised him to rest before being discharged. On the 10th of this month, the enteritis recurred. On the 19th, he gradually became comatose. Blood transfusions were ineffective, so he was moved back to his private residence in Happy Valley. He died at midnight on the 22nd. His mother is still alive, and he is survived by his wife, one son, and three daughters. The situation is bleak, relying on his former subordinates Ma Yuhang, Zhong Jingtang, and others to set up a funeral home to handle the funeral arrangements. (Central News Agency, 22nd)

Guangdong and Guangxi Authorities Promote Writing Brushes

(Guangzhou) The local authorities here are now seeking to resist the invasion of foreign stationery, as Chinese students now prefer to use pencils and fountain pens for writing. It is estimated that fountain pens imported into Guangzhou annually amount to a huge 600,000 yuan, while the old Chinese writing brushes have become almost obsolete. Education authorities are all regretting this. They are now seeking to request the provincial government to ban the use of fountain pens and order students to use writing brushes to write Chinese. It is reported that the Guangxi education authorities are also paying attention to this. An investigation shows that students in Guangxi Province use foreign-made pencils for 60 percent of writing, fountain pens for 28 percent, and Chinese writing brushes for only 12 percent. Therefore, the authorities are now discussing two measures: (1) School authorities must prohibit students from using pencils, steel pens, and fountain pens except when writing foreign languages. (2) Chinese letters, receipts, and all official documents must be written with Chinese paper and writing brushes. (Reuters, 22nd)

Fang's Troops Suddenly Occupy Huairou

The County Magistrate and Public Security Bureau Chief are Under Surveillance; Yin Tong Visits Chaisan to Negotiate Suppression Measures

A special dispatch from Peiping states that Fang Zhenwu, Ji Hongchang, Liu Guitang (including Zheng Guilin and Li Shouxin's troops), Tang Yulin, and others have new plans, intending to advance in three routes and attempt to infiltrate northern Hebei's Luan River region and eastern areas, join forces with the puppet army and bandits, and prepare for a major campaign. It is said that a certain country is behind this, providing all military expenses and weaponry from Chengde. Although Fang and his troops have begun military actions and occupied Huairou, due to the constraints of the Tanggu Truce Agreement, our side cannot dispatch troops. The situation of each party is described below:

Encirclement of Huairou

At 9:00 AM on the 20th, about 600 to 700 troops suddenly arrived in Huairou County, claiming to be Fang Zhenwu's forces. They set up posts inside and outside the city, only allowing merchants and civilians to leave the city but not to enter. On this day, Fang Zhenwu's forces, which had infiltrated Huairou County, had surrounded the county seat, cutting off transportation. The Public Security Bureau Chief of Gaoliying received a report in the afternoon that pedestrians could only reach Fengshankou, three miles from the city, where Fang's troops had set up posts, prohibiting passage. Fang's troops did not move south, so it is difficult to ascertain the situation inside the city. Fang Zhenwu and Ji Hongchang's troops previously fled east from Dushikou and gathered in the Fengning County area along the Rehe border, also mixed with the remnants of Zheng Guilin's troops, totaling about 5,000 or more. The day before yesterday, they infiltrated Hebei Province from Changyuankou in northern Huairou (Changyuankou is the only route between Huairou and Fengning). At 9:00 AM on the 20th, a company of cavalry from the vanguard of Fang Zhenwu's troops, about 100 or more, suddenly arrived at Huairou County. After hearing the alarm, the county government hurriedly ordered the closure of the four gates. Because Fang's cavalry moved quickly, they had not yet closed the gates. Fang's troops had already surrounded the county seat, and County Magistrate Xu Wenquan had not had time to withdraw. Transportation between Pinggu and Miyun was completely cut off after the afternoon of the 20th. According to people from Qiaozicun in Miyun, the cavalry team the day before yesterday entered Hebei Province from Fengning. Tang Yulin and Ji Hongchang's troops are also active near Changyuankou, severely checking pedestrians. Huairou is about 115 miles from northern Peiping.

He and Song Confer

Because a comprehensive plan for the aftermath in Chahar Province has not yet been fully agreed upon, the Chairman of Chahar Province, Song Zheyuan, has delayed his return to Chahar. After the adjournment of the regular meeting of the Peiping Military Branch on the 20th, Song again discussed with He Yingqin for a long time, until Song finally left at 1:00 PM. It is reported that the general principles for the Chahar situation have been largely agreed upon as follows: (1) Considering diplomatic relations, Fang Zhenwu and Ji Hongchang's infiltration into the Fengning area within the territory of Rehe will not be pursued for the time being. (2) National troops in eastern Chahar who have already arrived at their destinations will firmly defend their current positions and stop advancing. All other troops will temporarily suspend their departure to eastern Chahar. (3) Li Shouxin's bandit army in Guyuan has retreated to the Dolon area. All troops arriving in eastern Chahar will temporarily suspend guerrilla warfare. Chairman Chiang sent a telegram to Song, roughly stating that the Chahar region is extremely important, and Fang Zhenwu and Ji Hongchang's attitudes are ambiguous. He hopes that Song will return to Chahar as soon as possible to take charge of everything and asks for a reply regarding the date of his departure. After receiving the telegram, Song immediately replied, stating that the aftermath in Chahar is of great importance, and that he would do his best to shoulder the heavy responsibility. He has decided to depart on the afternoon of the horse day (21st) and hopes to receive instructions from time to time.

Japanese Planes Fly Over Shunyi

According to a telephone report from County Magistrate Su of Shunyi County Government at 11:30 AM today (21st), after Fang Zhenwu's troops occupied Huairou County on the 20th, the vanguard had only 600 to 700 people, but gradually increased, now totaling more than 2,000. After entering the city, they killed five members of the Public Security Team and confiscated all their weapons. They placed the County Magistrate, the Public Security Bureau Chief, and the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce under surveillance, restricting their freedom. Fang himself is currently stationed in the city, and his sentries have been placed in Nan Shicao, in the sixth district of Shunyi, seemingly with intentions of moving south. The county government is currently seeking instructions on how to respond. Furthermore, at 10:00 AM on the morning of the 21st, a Japanese plane flew from the north of Shunyi over Shunyi County, conducted a reconnaissance for a week, and then flew north again. Since the establishment of the Truce Agreement, Japanese planes have not come for a long time. This time, taking advantage of Fang Zhenwu's occupation of Huairou, Japanese planes came again for reconnaissance, which must have other intentions. The Military Branch held an emergency meeting this morning (21st) and discussed this matter. In addition to ordering certain troops to monitor the situation, measures to prevent Fang's troops from moving south were discussed. They also ordered the First Department to quickly draft appropriate measures for implementation. (Jin on the 21st)

The Situation of Entering the City

When Fang's troops arrived in Huairou on the morning of the 20th, the vanguard had a total of 600 to 700 people. There was a company of security guards stationed in the city, only about 100 people. Because the troops arrived suddenly, fearing conflict, they tightly closed the city gates. Because Fang's troops could not enter, they surrounded the city walls on all sides. Merchants and civilians, fearing further devastation in the city, sent representatives out of the city to negotiate with Wang Zhongfu's troops of Fang's army. Fang's only goal was to enter the city. The representatives of the merchants agreed to this and hoped that they would maintain order in the city after entering. In the afternoon, the city gates were opened, and after Fang's troops entered the city, they placed County Magistrate Xu Wenquan, the Public Security Bureau Chief, and the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce under strict surveillance. All security police were disarmed, and two or three people were shot and killed. Beforehand, Fang had reached a proper agreement with Ji, Liu, Tang, and the Japanese puppet forces. He also sent representatives to negotiate with bandit leaders in eastern Luan River, such as Lao Haozi. Liu Guitang also sent a unit to follow Fang's troops into the war zone. As of today (21st), Fang's troops have successively passed through Yong'anbao, and those moving south to Huairou have reached more than 2,000. Fang himself has also entered and stationed in Huairou City. The troops of Ji Hongchang, Tang Yulin, and Zheng Guilin are also continuing to advance. Ji's troops have also arrived at Yong'anbao.

Bandit Gangs Rampage

After Lao Haozi's bandit fleet occupied the Qinhuangdao area, they extorted hundreds of thousands from merchants and planned to enter the central war zone. Recently, it was reported that Fang Zhenwu's troops had entered Hebei Province and were eager to return to eastern Peiping to make contact with Fang. However, the merchants have not yet raised enough money. Lao Haozi was extremely angry and, starting on the 20th, set fire to villages, residences, and shops in the Qinhuangdao and Beidaihe area. According to those who came to Peiping on the Beining train this morning (21st), they saw smoke and fire spreading in the east when passing through Beidaihe last night, which was shocking. After burning the villages, the bandit troops planned to directly enter Sanhe and move towards Ji County. Because the war zone is a demilitarized zone as stipulated by the Tanggu Truce Agreement, the Japanese army in Rehe actually allowed Fang, Ji, and other troops to pass through and occupy the area, which is of great importance. Today (21st), a certain unit of the Ping Sui Line was ordered to monitor the edge of the war zone to prevent the situation from escalating.

Negotiating Suppression

At the same time, Yin Tong, a member of the Receiving Committee, negotiated with Chaisan, the Japanese military attaché stationed in Peiping, to find ways for both sides to suppress the bandit troops of Fang and others who infiltrated the war zone. Chaisan agreed and immediately telegraphed the Kwantung Army for instructions. If the other side does not have special intentions, they can agree to find a way to suppress them, and the situation may not escalate. However, the Japanese plane's reconnaissance over Shunyi today clearly shows their opinion. The Military Branch held a temporary meeting this morning (21st) and discussed this matter. In addition to ordering certain troops to monitor the situation, measures to prevent Fang's troops from moving south were discussed. They also ordered the First Department to quickly draft appropriate measures for implementation. (Jin, 21st)

Case to Continue Collection of Additional Customs Duty

Passed by the Legislative Yuan after Examination

At the general meeting of the Legislative Yuan on the morning of the 22nd, the Finance Committee reported on the examination of the case to continue collecting 5% additional customs duty, which was resolved and passed. The original presentation of the Finance Committee is recorded as follows: (Presented for reporting matters, according to the order of the Yuan, approved by the National Government Civil Service Office Letter No. 3441, transferred by the National Government Central Political Conference letter, approving the Executive Yuan's letter based on the Ministry of Finance's proposal to continue collecting 5% additional customs duty, which was submitted to the Finance Group for examination. The report stated that it is proposed to temporarily approve the extension of this additional 5% for eleven months within the 22nd year, and the amount to be collected will be included in the extraordinary budget and submitted to the government for prior implementation. When the Legislative Yuan is in session, it will be submitted for ratification. After deliberation by this conference, it was resolved to pass it according to the examination opinions and sent to the government for reference and compliance. It was ordered to forward it for compliance, etc. In addition to replying and ordering the government to order the Executive Yuan to forward it to the Ministry of Finance for compliance, etc., the original letter should be copied and sent for reference, etc. This committee complied on the 7th of this month and convened the sixth meeting of the third session to submit it for examination. It was resolved that the case of continuing to collect 5% additional customs duty has already been ordered by the government to the Executive Yuan to forward it to the Ministry of Finance for compliance. The case has been implemented first, and it is requested that the extension be approved for eleven months, with a fixed period. It is proposed to grant ratification. Is this appropriate? Please review and submit it to the general meeting for public decision.)

(2) To request assistance from all parties for the Yellow River floods in Shaanxi and Gansu, as the disaster situation in the counties along the Yellow River in Shaanxi and Gansu is dire and in urgent need of relief. (September 21st)

Sun Tonggang Flies to Wuhan, Warmly Welcomed by All Sectors, Will Fly to Hunan in the Coming Days

A dispatch from Hankou states that aviator Sun Tonggang, accompanied by his classmate Wang Zuwen, flew the "Aviation to Save the Nation" aircraft west from Anqing on the 21st and arrived in Wuhan at 12:30 PM, landing at the Wangjiadun airfield. About 5,000 people from various agencies, organizations, schools, and all sectors of the public welcomed them at the airfield. The enthusiastic situation was unprecedented. When Sun's plane arrived in Wuhan, it circled the three towns of Wuhan for a week. The 4th Aviation Team dispatched planes to welcome them, performing various technical demonstrations in the air for about half an hour before descending amidst cheers. After Sun and Wang got off the plane, two young female students each presented a bouquet of flowers, which Sun accepted with a smile. He then stood on the plane and gave a speech to the crowd, roughly saying: (I studied in Germany, but my accomplishments are not deep. This time, I flew back to the country to promote aviation to save the nation and arouse public attention. I am truly ashamed to receive such a warm welcome from the people. Today, I took off from Anqing and encountered many Chinese merchant ships carrying passengers. I circled the ship, and when they saw the four characters "Aviation to Save the Nation" on the plane, they all clapped and welcomed us. It can be seen that the people have awakened). After the speech, Wu Shao-shu, a member of the Municipal Party Department, gave a reply. Then, they went to the Pacific Hotel for rest. Sun also gave a speech to reporters, detailing his return from Germany, crossing the continent, and the nationwide flight. He will stay in Wuhan for three days and then go to Changsha, and then transfer to Zhumadian, Zhengzhou, Luoyang, Kaifeng, Baoding, Taiyuan, Datong, Peiping, Tianjin, Zhangjiakou and other places. Sun also said: (The motive for this flight is entirely to promote aviation to save the nation, and I am grateful for my father's earnest advice and the active urging of my classmates. The expenses are entirely self-funded. I hope the press will expand the publicity of aviation to save the nation to save the country from danger). In the afternoon, Sun visited the headquarters of the Pacification Commissioner's Office, the Provincial Government, and the Provincial and Municipal Party Departments. In the evening, he attended a banquet hosted by the Municipal Party Department. The location of the welcome meeting of all sectors was originally scheduled for the New Market, but has now been changed to the Guangming Grand Theater, scheduled to be held at 10 AM on the 22nd. According to Wang, (Sun's plane has only 80 horsepower. The planes used in our country have reached 120 horsepower, and foreigners need hundreds of horsepower to fly long distances. Now, Mr. Sun is using a plane with 80 horsepower to accomplish this unprecedented feat, and the achievements are truly amazing. Because of our relationship as classmates, I am traveling with him. Next spring, we will go to Germany together to seek further study.) (21st)

Completion of Lingshan River Bridge on Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway

Also Opened to Traffic on the 21st

The newly built Lingshan River Bridge of the Jin-Yu section of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway is located at Jimingyan outside the South Gate of Longyou, spanning the Lingshan River, with seven spans, more than 460 feet long. The piers of the bridge are built of concrete, and the bridge beams and deck are made of steel, with a total weight of approximately 200 tons. The bridge piers and deck engineering were all contracted by the Shanghai Yangtze Construction Company. The steel materials used were specially ordered from famous German factories, with a total cost of more than 110,000 yuan. It was completed and opened to traffic on the 21st of this month. It is reported that the bridge piers are built on red soft stone 13-14 feet below the water surface, and the foundation waterproofing project was extremely difficult. The bridge deck riveting and hoisting work was completed in only one month, demonstrating the rich experience and adequate measures of the contracting company.

Songjiang

Danger at Jinshanwei Seawall

The Jinshanwei seawall in Punan suddenly experienced strong southeast winds and a sharp rise in sea levels around 3:00 PM on the 18th. In the evening, the wind shifted north and was also very strong. At night, the tide nearly reached the car road. A bamboo raft was washed onto the seawall surface. Fortunately, fishing boats had already docked at Qijiadun to avoid accidents. A fishing boat belonging to a certain Mr. Bei in Beiku disappeared that night, and its whereabouts are unknown. Several fishermen are missing, and their lives and deaths are uncertain. Waves have been rising and falling for days, breaking countless tree piles, and the seawall body has newly collapsed for hundreds of feet. The dangerous project at Longzhu Nunnery, which was repaired last year, has not yet been properly constructed. It is fortunate that it was not affected by the disaster this time. Speakers say that the tide is large during the minor flood season, but the current is still slow. If the winds and tides rise again in mid-August, the three counties of Songjiang, Fengxian, and Jinshan may become a swamp. Therefore, coastal residents are very worried.

Xi's Murder Case Has Been Publicly Prosecuted

In the tragic deaths of Hua Yang Overseas Chinese Xi Weiquan and his wife, the Public Security Bureau arrested Xu Guanxiang and Shen Ahe, and the Water Patrol Team also captured Wu Zixiang. It was discovered that the deceased's younger brother, Wei Sheng, hated him for occupying the inheritance and plotted murder out of hatred. The suspects Xi Weisheng and his concubine Song Xiaomei were arrested. After repeated investigations, Prosecutor Zhu has filed a public prosecution, prosecuting Shen Ahe under Article 1, Clause 12 of the Law on Punishing Bandits and prosecuting Xi Weisheng, Song Xiaomei, and Xu Guanxiang under the provisions of the Criminal Law on conspiracy to commit murder. Wu Zixiang also has a kidnapping case and is being prosecuted under the Law on Punishing Bandits. It is reported that Xi Weisheng and Song Xiaomei have hired Lu Longxiang as their defense lawyer.

Suzhou Fishermen's Association Appeals for Fishmongers

The Wu County Business Tax Bureau notified all fish businesses to collect business tax on behalf of the fishmongers. The fish businesses believe that the fishmongers in Wu County are all poor and have no ability to bear the business tax. Therefore, they appealed to the Wu County Fishermen's Association for relief. The association specially sent a telegram to the Suzhou Provincial Government and the Department of Finance yesterday (22nd), requesting that the bureau be ordered to stop the tax collection in order to maintain the livelihoods of the poor.

Resolution of Business Tax Dispute in Changzhou

Since the Wuyi Business Tax Bureau implemented the investigation in the autumn, various industries have strongly opposed the account checking. The dispute has lasted for a long time. Recently, County Magistrate Cai took the initiative to mediate, and after several consultations, there have been some signs of progress. The County Chamber of Commerce also convened a meeting of various industries yesterday and resolved the following matters: (1) The business tax of each business from the autumn of this year will be increased by 10% based on the original amount in the first half of the year. (2) The autumn taxes must be paid directly to the tax bureau by the businesses before October 5th. (3) Special circumstances in the oil, grain, and yarn industries are earnestly requested to be reduced or exempted, which will be forwarded immediately.

Two Robber-Criminals Executed by Firing Squad

The Wu County Administration learned from the County Public Security Bureau and the Detective Team that they had captured and escorted two criminals, Zhang Chaxing and Zhang Zhaohai, who confessed to their involvement in robbing boats near Xuantang. They were sentenced to death and presented to the Provincial Government for approval. County Magistrate Cai immediately sent police officers on the afternoon of the 21st to bring the two criminals to the case, verify their identities, and bind them to the Fengweidun execution ground for execution by firing squad.

Repercussions of the Wuxi Lime Guild's Oppression of Members

The Lime Boat Industry Guild in this county was established in 1919. Due to incompetent management and corruption, disputes have arisen repeatedly. In July of this year, the guild members Gu Rongpei and others accused the guild of coercion, extortion, and embezzlement of public funds, and reported it to the County Party Department and the County Court Procuratorate. The 88th meeting of the County Party Department resolved to revoke the guild's permit and ordered the county to dissolve it. On the morning of the 7th of this month, a lime boat belonging to guild member An Xinbao transported more than 190 loads of lime from Yixing to the county. When unloading at Dongting, guild committee member Yu Genxiang and others led a large group of people to the scene, accusing the boat of violating the guild rules and arbitrarily departing, causing a great dispute. The boat owner An Xinbao claimed that when he loaded the lime in Wuxi, he registered with the guild as required and did not violate the guild rules. Even if there was a violation of the guild rules, the industry guild had no right to seize the boat. He accused the guild of illegal behavior, resembling that of thugs, and specially submitted a petition on the guild's misdeeds and the seizure of the boat. He also attached various evidence and submitted it to Chairman Jiang of Jiangxi, the National Government of Nanjing, the Central Party Department, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, the Zhenjiang Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, and the County Party Department and County Government of this county, requesting relief. The original text is very long, and the main points are: (1) Listing the guild's clever establishment of names and coercion and extortion. (2) Listing the facts of embezzlement of public funds and seeking private gain and malpractice. (3) Detailing the seizure of boats, goods, and silver dollars. (4) The guild's organization fundamentally violates laws and regulations, requesting a clear investigation and disbandment. Before one wave has subsided, another has risen. Yesterday, a lime boat belonging to a non-member, Hua Yongfa, was also unloading goods outside the West Gate when guild committee member Ling Xinbao and others led a large group of people and police officers from the 4th Branch of the Public Security Bureau to seize the boat and detain the boatmen, submitting them to the County Public Security Bureau. Ling Fenghao, the executive director of the Lime Boat Guild, voluntarily turned himself in for questioning. After Wu, the section chief, opened the court for questioning, Hua Yongfa testified that he was not a member of the guild, and the guild's illegal actions were an obstruction of freedom, requesting strict punishment according to law. Ling Fenghao's testimony was evasive. The result of the court's order was that Hua Yongfa was ordered to return, Ling Fenghao was released on bail, and the lime boat was returned to Hua Yongfa. After the order was completed, Ling Fenghao found the Tang Hengtai Lime Company in the Big City Bridge to bail him out of the bureau. It was already 12:00 AM. It is now reported that Hua Yongfa has officially sued the court for obstruction of freedom.

Successful Resolution of Kidnapping Case in Wangjia Village, Danyang

One evening last month, several bandits armed with pistols and sharp weapons broke into the home of farmer Wang Mingdeng in Wangjia Village, in the western countryside. They searched the inner rooms extensively, but were still not satisfied. Before leaving, they kidnapped his young son and left a note demanding a huge ransom, which was not successful. Now the kidnappers in this case have been intercepted by the Inland River Patrol Fleet of the Jiangsu Provincial Police Headquarters in Wuxi. A boat was seized on the spot, and the kidnappers Tao Shaoqin, Chen Xiaolong, Chen Guangyu, and Shao Qiaoxiao were arrested and two pistols were seized. They were taken back to the headquarters for interrogation. They confessed to the kidnapping case in Danyang. Now police have been sent to escort the criminals to Danyang for trial.

Dismantling a Counterfeit Cigarette Machine

The local branch of the Cigarette Company learned that someone was counterfeiting various brands of cigarettes, such as Pyramid and Stone Seal, in a house next to the electric light factory outside the North Gate, and selling them on the market. They reported it to the Security Branch, which went to dismantle the counterfeit machine and arrested the counterfeiters Gong Shaofu and Xi Fenglin. They found various counterfeit machines and counterfeit stone seal cigarettes, which have now been sent to the County Bureau for interrogation.

Two Well-Known Bandits of Nantong-Ruga Executed by Firing Squad

Tao Dong and Yan Sui, two well-known bandits in Nantong-Ruga, committed numerous crimes. Last month, they were captured by the Pingchao Police Regiment and escorted to the Nantong County Government for interrogation. They confessed to robbing, arson, and murder and were identified by the victims. After the trial, they were sentenced to death. The Provincial Government was requested for instructions, and an order was received on the 21st to escort the two criminals to the scene of the crime for execution by firing squad.

Statistics of Flood Losses in Chongming

Chongming is surrounded by the sea on all sides, and the ground is very low. Usually, the tides are controlled by the people's dikes. The dikes along the northern coast were completely destroyed by the autumn wind last winter, causing huge losses. Unfortunately, the wind came again last night, and the northern parts of the first, second, third, fourth, fifth, and seventh districts were submerged again, and the situation was twice as severe as last winter. The repaired dikes were destroyed again, and the unrepaired ones drove straight in, causing the water to flood. The city and the sea dikes of Chenghai were damaged in more than 40 sections. Details are still under investigation due to the disruption of transportation. The County Relief Association has sent personnel to distribute relief supplies. The first statistics of the disaster are as follows: The disaster area is 695 square li, more than 200 li of dikes were destroyed, more than 6,200 houses were washed away, 208 people died, 22,165 people were affected, and 274,740 mu of farmland were affected.

Director Xu of Qingjiang Leaves Pu to Return to Yang

Xu Dingkang, Director of the Jiangbei Canal Engineering Bureau, previously heard frequent reports of floods and breaches of the Yellow River in Lu and Yu. He noted that the waters were flowing into the Weishan and Zhaoyang lakes at the junction of Jiangsu and Shandong and were about to flow into the Central Canal, causing a dangerous situation. He specifically telegraphed the counties in northern Jiangsu, ordering them to repair any breaches of the Central Canal, the Outer Canal, the abandoned Yellow River, and the Six Tang Dikes, and to remove any dams. He also personally led Secretary Shen Baojun and others to Huaiyin to supervise the situation and send personnel to various counties to inspect and assist in the repairs. Now that the Yellow River water has receded and the work is not as urgent as before, he specifically ordered the Huai-Pi section's engineering office to be dismantled first on the 19th. He concluded all work on that day and hired a sailboat to attach it to the back of the Xin Chun special ship before departing from Huai and returning to Yang.

Adultery in Jiashan Leads to Murder

Fei Qingting, a farmer from Luxu Township, has a daughter who is unmarried. She was coveted by Zhang Wuguan, a neighbor, but was unable to succeed due to Fei's strict family rules. The other day, Fei's family had a funeral, and Wuguan thought he had an opportunity. He used the name of mourning to have an affair with the daughter. Her uncle discovered the affair and gathered workers to capture the shameless man and woman. At that time, they used hoes and sticks, causing the adulterer to be beaten to death. The matter was learned by Wuguan's family, who rushed to Fei's house to make trouble, and at the same time reported to the County Government for inspection.

Thorough Investigation of Illegal Sale of Military Mountain Land in Pinghu

It has been repeatedly heard that unscrupulous people from Liangzhuang and Changshan townships in Zha Pu are stealing and selling land in Baoshan. Even strategically important land is being sold to foreigners. Recently, Li Chunhe, Fang Tianfu, Fang Chunrong, and others sold the military mountain land of Yunding Mountain to a certain Westerner. The top of this mountain is flat. It is said that Emperor Qin Shihuang tested his sword there, and the mountaintop was cut off and fell into the sea. The Coffin Reef in the sea has repeatedly damaged ships, and it is said to be the top of this mountain. It is recorded in local chronicles and is considered a scenic spot. After the news of the illegal sale spread, local people requested the county government to thoroughly investigate. The county government, based on the report, secretly ordered the Zha Pu district office to arrest the perpetrators. Today, the two suspects, Li and Fang, have been arrested and sent to the county for interrogation. It is said that more than twenty people are involved.

Verdict in the Hangzhou Case of Brutal Murder of a Farmhand

Qi Zhongbao, a farmer residing at No. 6, Kuoshi Ban Caoshe, West Lake, along with his wife, Xu, etc., used a kitchen knife to brutally murder their farmhand, Shen Afa, with thirteen cuts, killing him. They then buried the body in a vegetable garden to cover up the crime. However, the incident was revealed by a short-term worker, Qi Demao. The local police station exhumed the body and brought the perpetrators to court for trial. The investigation has now concluded, and the verdict was announced yesterday. Qi Zhongbao was sentenced to life imprisonment for premeditated murder. His wife, Xu, was sentenced to ten years of imprisonment. Qi Demao, the short-term worker, was sentenced to one year and three months of imprisonment. The son, A Mao, was declared not guilty.

Seven Robbers Captured in the Chao Mountain Arson Case

In March of this year, a robbery and arson occurred at Daming Temple in Chao Mountain, Tangqi, Hangzhou County, resulting in the burning of the temple buildings and the death of the abbot. Currently, the local public security bureau has captured seven suspects: Shen Bingtang, Zhu Agui, Zhou Aquan, Zhu Guichun, Shi Yunkui, Shi Atuo, and the female bandit Shi Zhang. They have also confiscated firearms and stolen goods. Yesterday, they were sent to the Hangzhou District Court for investigation. The suspects gave evasive testimonies and were ordered to be detained pending further proceedings.

New Education Bureau Chief in Xiaoshan Takes Office

Lou Qingyuan, the chief of the Xiaoshan County Education Bureau, was ordered to be transferred to the provincial government. His vacancy will be filled by Cheng Fenglai, the chief of the Lanxi County Education Bureau. The new Chief Cheng arrived in Xiaoshan today (the 21st) to take office. All internal staff of the bureau have been replaced accordingly.

Girl Crushed to Death in House Collapse Due to Wind and Rain

The house of a villager, Miao Agou, located next to the Chen clan ancestral hall outside the East Gate Hualang Bridge, collapsed due to years of disrepair and dilapidated condition on the night of the 20th. Miao and his wife were awakened from their sleep and found themselves amidst the rubble. Most tragically, their three-year-old daughter was crushed and killed by the collapsed debris.

Major Fire at Hongsheng Warehouse in Ningbo Jiangdong

At around 5:00 AM yesterday morning (the 20th), a fire broke out at the Hongsheng warehouse, No. 53, Muhang Road, Jiangdong, Ningbo, due to the Fuyang ash stored in the warehouse dissolving due to tidal water. When the Jiangdong Yilong fire brigades arrived at the scene after hearing the alarm, the fire had already broken through the roof and was impossible to approach. Furthermore, there were many oils in the warehouse, making it extremely difficult to extinguish. All the Yilong brigades from the city center were unable to pass due to the old Jiang Bridge being broken by the hurricane. Only the Laian Association and the Linan Association managed to hire boats to cross the river and assist in the firefighting. It took two hours to extinguish the fire. It is estimated that dozens of businesses, including Chengtai Jiang Youhang, were burned, with losses amounting to around 100,000 yuan. Also, at 11:00 PM last night, a fire broke out in the warehouse of the World Bookstore in Lane 44, Cuiya Street, Ningbo. It took half an hour to extinguish the fire. The books stored in the World Bookstore warehouse were worth over 10,000 yuan and were completely burned. Fortunately, there was fire insurance, so the loss was relatively small. Several other burned houses included the Shirui Ji Cloth Store, with significant losses.

Gradually Eliminating Opium and Banditry in Huizhou

The Huizhou region of southern Anhui borders Jiangxi Province, and the area of Wuyuan County, which belongs to Huizhou, was partially occupied by bandits and communists. After Chairman Jiang of the Military Affairs Commission designated it as the Tenth District of Anhui and dispatched Administrative Inspector and Commander Liu Cheng粹 to lead troops to suppress them, the bandits were driven back. However, scattered bandits hid within the territory, taking advantage of the situation to kidnap, rob, and sell opium, acting sporadically. The remaining evils were quite rampant, and the people of Huizhou suffered greatly. Commissioner Liu, on the one hand, vigorously implemented the autonomous system, established Baojia (household registration) and trained local militia to cut off the bandits' trails. On the other hand, he secretly deployed detectives, arresting and executing the notorious bandit leaders and master criminals involved in the production and sale of red pills (opium pills). Currently, opium rehabilitation centers, unemployment relief centers, beggar education centers, and national goods promotion venues are being established in various counties to provide outlets for those addicted to opium and the unemployed, while also employing veteran scholars and celebrities to lecture everywhere to influence people's hearts. Deputy Security Commander Wang Han is brave and resolute, providing effective assistance. Therefore, the scourge of opium and banditry in Huizhou has gradually been eliminated, and the people of Huizhou can breathe a sigh of relief for a while. The local legal entities and gentry of each county have separately submitted requests to the Military Affairs Commission, the Administrative Council, the Provincial Government, and the Government of Anhui for recognition of Liu and Wang.

Local News

Mayor Wu Personally Inspected Wind-Damaged Seawalls Yesterday

The West Seawall is Nearing Completion, While the East Seawall Remains at Risk

According to the Central News Agency, during the two recent typhoons that hit this city, they coincided with high tides, causing raging winds and flooding, which surged ashore, damaging the seawalls, destroying crops, and causing significant losses. Various districts have successively requested relief. The Municipal Bureau of Public Works immediately dispatched personnel to repair the seawalls day and night. The West Seawall will be completed today, while the East Seawall remains at risk. Regarding the disaster-stricken areas, the Municipal Government has ordered the three bureaus of Social Affairs, Land, and Finance to quickly devise relief measures. Yesterday morning, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, accompanied by Shen Yi, Director of the Bureau of Public Works, and others, personally inspected the situation and provided instructions. The details are as follows:

The East Seawall Remains at Risk, While Repairs to the West Seawall are Nearing Completion

Since the first typhoon struck this city on September 1st, many seawalls have been damaged, and the work of emergency repairs has not yet been completed. The second typhoon and rainstorm struck Shanghai again on September 18th, causing the repair work to be damaged again. The breaches caused by the first typhoon have increased. According to Dai Erjing, the chief of the Seawall Section of the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, the East Seawall (the coastal area of Gaoqiao District) was more severely damaged than the West Seawall (the Baoshan-Wusong area). The West Seawall was damaged at Wumufeng, with a breach of 14 feet in length and eight layers of stone slabs washed away. That section of the seawall is entirely stone, making the construction relatively solid, with wooden piles on the outside. The dangerous situation is less severe than that of the East Seawall. After the danger occurred, the Bureau of Public Works immediately hired workers to repair the breaches to prevent further disasters. The repair work can be completed tomorrow (i.e., today). The East Seawall (the coastal area of Gaoqiao District) is entirely earthen. When the first typhoon struck Shanghai, the seawall was damaged for five kilometers, including Moan, Zhangjiazhai, Qijiacun, Tangjiaci, Longwangmiao, and Yangjiazhai. According to statistics, the repair work required more than 600,000 English feet. After the Bureau inspected the situation, it invited bids, and the Xiehe Company was contracted to build it. Before the construction had been underway for long, the second typhoon struck again, destroying eight or nine tenths of the built work. The damaged seawall was even more severely damaged two days after being attacked by the wind and waves. After the second typhoon, the Bureau immediately dispatched personnel to hire workers to repair the breaches. At that time, because both the outside and inside of the dike were flooded, there was no way to obtain soil, and it was impossible to proceed for a while. Therefore, they are currently trying to pump out the accumulated water inside the dike. The Xiehe Company has already dispatched an additional 400 workers to assist in the rescue. The Municipal Government has allocated 50,000 yuan for emergency rescue funds. It is estimated that the entire repair project will require more than 500,000 yuan.

Significant Damage to Farmland, the Municipal Government is Seeking Relief

The reporter inquired with villagers in various disaster-stricken areas. According to them, all the villagers along the seawall were most severely affected because they had not prepared in advance and were not able to obtain timely relief afterward. The residents' houses were almost entirely washed down by the seawater, and livestock were also harmed, which was heartbreaking to see. According to experienced farmers, this year's cotton crop, although not very abundant, was expected to yield 100 catties per acre. After this disaster, seventy or eighty percent of the crop was lost. The rice crop was expected to yield more than 500 catties, but now forty or fifty percent of the crop has been lost. Therefore, the losses incurred this time are truly staggering. After receiving reports that a typhoon was coming to Shanghai, the Municipal Government immediately ordered the relevant bureaus to prepare for emergency repairs and provide relief. Currently, disaster-stricken areas such as Wusong, Yinxiang, and Gaoqiao have successively submitted reports to the Municipal Government requesting prompt relief. The Municipal Government immediately transferred the matter to the Land, Finance, and Social Affairs Bureaus to jointly discuss relief measures. The measures will be divided into two types: emergency relief and gradual relief. The bureaus have sent personnel to the disaster-stricken areas to conduct on-the-spot inspections and provide emergency relief at any time and place. As for gradual relief measures, such as exempting land taxes or providing disaster relief loans, the bureaus will discuss them before submitting them to the Municipal Government for approval.

Mayor Wu Went to Wusong Yesterday to Inspect Seawall Construction

Mayor Wu paid unusual attention to the seawalls of the city, which related to the life and property of the entire city. He went to Wusong yesterday morning at 9 a.m. with Director of the Bureau of Public Works Shen Yi, Secretary of the Municipal Government Zhang Tingrong, Chief of the First Section Li Dachao, Chief Xu of the Second Section of the Bureau of Public Works, Chief Dai Erjing of the Seawall Section, and others to inspect the seawalls and direct and supervise the repairs. The visit lasted about three hours. On the way back, he went to the central area of the city for inspections. Only after 1 p.m. he returned to the Municipal Government in Fenglinqiao for a rest.

Song Ziwen Returned to Shanghai from Nanjing This Morning

Negotiating Methods for Cotton Merchants and Mills to Purchase and Pay for American Cotton

Minister of Finance Song Ziwen went to Nanjing on official business last Sunday. As the first batch of American cotton is about to arrive in port, he and his wife Zhang Leyi and daughter took the customs patrol ship "Liuxing" (Meteor) to Shanghai from Nanjing at 11 a.m. yesterday to negotiate methods for cotton merchants and mills to purchase and pay for American cotton and other issues. The ship is expected to arrive in port at 10 a.m. this morning.

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce Convenes the National Production Conference

The Opening Cannot Be Held on October 1st

According to the Central News Agency, news of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce convening the National Production Conference has been frequently reported in Nanjing and Shanghai. It was set to be held in Shanghai on October 1st. However, according to information obtained by the Central News Agency reporter, various factories in Shanghai, aware of the backwardness of domestic production, which is worsening year by year, believe that if measures are not taken to save it, the future will be dire. Therefore, they have requested the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to quickly convene the National Production Conference. Chen Gongbo, the Minister of Industry and Commerce, also realized that saving the backward production was urgent, so he invited representatives from factories in Shanghai to the Ministry to discuss and decided to convene the National Factory Representatives Conference in the short term. However, the date and location have not been decided, as considerable time is still needed for preparation. It is not confirmed that the opening will be on October 1st.

All Institutions in This City Fly Flags at Half-Mast in Mourning

Yesterday was the third anniversary of the death of the late President of the Executive Yuan, Tan Yankai. All institutions affiliated with the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government flew flags at half-mast to express mourning.

Mayor Wu Inspects Police This Morning

Participating in the Inspection are More than 1,800 Troops at the Nanshi Public Gymnasium at 9:00 AM

Wen Hongen, the Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, in order to implement the police training program and rectify discipline, had originally planned to invite Mayor Wu to inspect the city's police on the 20th. Inspection Procedure

The inspection procedure is as follows: (1) Speech; (2) Parade; (3) Pass in Review; (4) Company Formation Drill; (5) Platoon Combat Drill; (6) Machine Gun Company Formation Drill; (7) Broadsword Exercise; (8) Boxing Exercise; (9) Photography; (10) Conclusion.

Participating Troops

The security of the venue will be handled by Captain Lu Ying of the Detective Squad, leading a large number of detectives, and District Chief Li of the Second District, dispatching police officers to maintain order around the venue.

Du Yong and Others Telegraphically Request Relief for the Fishing Industry

Adding a Special Project to the Economic Commission

According to the Central News Agency, Du Yong and 28 other fishermen and aquatic researchers from various provinces, including Shanghai, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shandong, Hebei, Guangdong, and Fujian, telegraphed the Central Government yesterday, requesting that measures be taken to relieve fishing villages and that a special project for relieving the fishing industry be added to the National Economic Commission. The original telegram is recorded as follows: Nanjing: Sent to the Standing Committee of the Central Party Headquarters, the Central Political Conference, Chairman Lin of the National Government, President Wang of the Executive Yuan, President Sun of the Legislative Yuan, the Military Affairs Commission (transferred to Commander Jiang in Jiujiang), Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance, Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the National Economic Commission, the Construction Commission, the Rural Reconstruction Committee, and all concerned: Fishing villages in our country account for a large proportion of rural areas in coastal provinces. In recent years, they have been on the verge of bankruptcy, with fishing grounds being oppressed by Japanese ships and fishermen turning to banditry. The aquaculture industry in freshwater areas is also an important sideline for rural areas. Without measures to relieve them, it is insufficient to seek revitalization. It is hoped that the Central Government will select and employ fishery experts to join committees such as the Rural Reconstruction Committee or establish a national fishery improvement committee to control the entire country, and add a special project for relieving the fishing industry to the National Economic Commission to carefully formulate plans, determine funding, and implement revitalization. We respectfully request your approval to comfort the people. Shanghai: Du Yong, Lin Kanghou, Fang Jiaobo, Chen Chunshou, Wang Defa; Jiangsu: Hou Chaohai, Wang Wentai, Feng Limin, Chen Hanyu, Zhang Guizun, Qian Cangshuo, Wang Jue; Zhejiang: Wu Zhenbi, Zhang Chuanbao, Hu Juntong, Jin Shao, Chen Moulang; Hebei: Zhang Yuandi, Zheng Zichen, Liu Lun; Guangdong: Chen Tongbai, Bao Yingzhong, Huang Zhengyan, Zeng Guangqing; Fujian: Wu Yi, Zhang Rongchang, Cheng Yiyue, Zhang Huihuang; Shandong: Li Anren. Together, we respectfully present this petition.

Investigating and Explaining the Reasons for the Tide Surging Ashore

Surging ashore is Due to the Gradual Silting Up of the Yangtze River Estuary, Which Will Require a New Channel, Causing the River Water to Back Up into the Huangpu River. Yesterday, the reporter questioned Charlie, the Chief Engineer of the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau. According to him, the silting up of the Yangtze River Estuary will certainly raise the water level. However, if this were the only result, the residents of Shanghai would need to raise the roads and foundations of their houses by one or two feet in about two hundred years. The recent surges ashore were entirely caused by the coincidence of the typhoon and high tides. Although the water level of the Yangtze River Estuary is often two or three feet higher in the summer and autumn than in the winter and spring, the impact is minimal, and Shanghai will not often experience surges ashore.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Replies to the Two Associations on Returning Donation Receipts

The Party and Government Institutions Have Approved the Method and Should Request Various Groups to Handle the Matter Themselves

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to the Northeastern Volunteer Army Support Association and the Former Shanghai Local Maintenance Association, stating, "Regarding the unanimous demand from public opinion in this city to investigate the national salvation donations collected by various organizations, this Chamber of Commerce proposed that the Party and government institutions, which were not involved in the collection of funds, should dispatch personnel to thoroughly investigate the matter to demonstrate seriousness. We submitted reports to the Municipal Government and the Municipal Party Headquarters for approval and inquired with your Association for your opinions. We received a reply that the account books and receipts would be sent to our Chamber first. However, after reviewing this case, our Chamber first received instructions from the Municipal Government stating that it had ordered the Bureau of Social Affairs to investigate and handle the matter. Today, we also saw a report stating that the Municipal Party Headquarters' Notice No. 92 stated that all national salvation organizations should send the accounts and receipts of the donations they handled to the Shanghai All-Circles National Salvation Donation Investigation Committee for review within one week. As the method has been approved and the deadline is limited, the 50th Standing Committee Meeting of our Chamber decided to return the sent receipts to the various national salvation organizations and ask them to handle the matter themselves, without our Chamber transferring them, to comply with the regulations. The receipts that have not been sent to our Chamber will also be replied to in this manner. Accordingly, the receipt books and records are sent back with this letter. Please take note."

The Japanese Ship Changchun Maru

Collision with the Tunan Ship Undergoing Arbitration

The Board of Directors Has Submitted a Request to the Ministry to Establish an Arbitration Tribunal to Impartially Arbitrate

After the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Tunan ship was sunk by the Changchun Maru, the Japanese ignored the matter, and the Maritime Court in Dalian even announced that the sinking of the Tunan ship was not the fault of the Japanese ship. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company believes that this case has been delayed for a long time, and the Japanese have adopted a policy of ignoring it, resulting in huge losses for the company. After consultation, it was decided to submit a request to the Ministry to submit the Tunan case to arbitration to clarify responsibilities and seek a solution. The company's memorial requesting arbitration has been submitted to the Ministry by the Board of Directors. The details of the case are as follows:

Unilateral Judgment by the Japanese Side

The Dalian Maritime Court has now announced that after the trial of the collision between the Changchun Maru and the Tunan ship, the fault was not with the Japanese ship. This ruling has been notified to the Dalian Shipping Company. However, the Maritime Court rashly announced a judgment based on a unilateral request, which is not legal or reasonable in fact and naturally has no effect.

Repeated Negotiations Ineffective

After the Tunan ship sank, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company investigated the truth of the case. After a detailed investigation, it was determined that the fault lay with the Japanese ship Changchun Maru, and conclusive evidence was obtained. The company sent a letter to the Dalian Shipping Company based on the facts and reasons for serious negotiations, but the Japanese ignored the letter several times. The bow of the Changchun Maru that was damaged in the collision has now been repaired, renamed the Qingdao Maru, and continues to operate between Dalian, Qingdao, and Shanghai as usual. Recently, it has used the unilateral judgment of the Dalian Maritime Bureau as an excuse to disregard the serious responsibilities of sinking the Tunan ship, including the deaths of crew and passengers and the loss of cargo.

Submitting a Request for Arbitration

General Manager Liu Hongsheng has reported the process of this case to the Board of Directors, requesting that this case be submitted to arbitration. The Board of Directors passed the resolution and immediately submitted a memorial to the Ministry, stating, "The case of the Tunan ship being sunk by the Changchun Maru off Chengshanjiao, Shandong, has been thoroughly investigated by our company, and the responsibility for the accident should be attributed to the Japanese ship. However, the shipping company has ignored our company's repeated negotiations. If we file a lawsuit with the court, not only is there a jurisdictional issue, but also the precedent of the Japanese mail ship Ryuno Maru sinking the Xinkang ship was ignored, making it difficult to handle the matter through legal means. If we file a lawsuit in the Japanese court, it would be even more difficult to achieve a satisfactory result due to geographic and political constraints. The only option is to conduct arbitration, hire impartial personnel, and impartially arbitrate to ensure that the responsible party bears full responsibility and that losses are compensated. This memorial has been sent to the Ministry and will be processed upon approval."

Planned to be Conducted in Shanghai

Regarding the progress of the arbitration, the reporter inquired with Qian of the company. It is likely that an arbitration committee will be established in Shanghai, with experts in navigation and impartial individuals hired by both the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Dalian Shipping Company to form an arbitration tribunal. However, neither the Chinese nor Japanese sides may add members to the committee to ensure impartiality. The arbitration tribunal will summon the shipowners and crew of both parties, conduct an impartial inquiry, and determine the responsibility for the case. The company will send a letter to the Dalian Shipping Company to jointly discuss hiring experts and negotiate the number of members of the arbitration committee after the Ministry's approval is received, and then transfer the entire case to the arbitration tribunal for arbitration.
