A Record of Heroes and Heroines Competing on the Track

Dong Shuzhao Sets a New National Record in the 800m

Qian Hangsu Overcomes Three Obstacles, but Her Performance is Diminished

Su Xiaoru Wins the 100m on Opening Day

The first event to be decided was the 100m. All eight athletes who qualified for the final were determined to win. Therefore, around 1 o'clock, they all did light exercises around the track to warm up their muscles and bones. When the starter, Jiang Xiangqing, gave the order, the runners each took their positions on the track. The strong athlete, Cheng Jinguang, was too eager to win and rushed out of the starting line before the gun fired, which caused him to be called back by the starter. On the second start, Su Xiaoru had the fastest start, and Hao Chunde had the slowest start. All the way, Su Xiaoru was always in front, and Cheng and Hao were chasing closely behind. When they reached the finish line, Cheng was just a shoulder behind, finishing second, and Hao was another shoulder behind, finishing third. Xue Jianqiu came in fourth. After the race, photographers scrambled to take pictures. Xiaoru had a smiling face and politely greeted everyone with one hand, showing humility and courtesy.

Shuzhao Sets a New National Record in the 800m. Following the 100m

The next final was the 800m. There were eight runners at the start. After the gun fired, Dong Shuzhao took the lead and seized the inner lane. In the second lap, Li Yanxiang gradually caught up with considerable strength, only two or three meters behind Dong. Spectators all thought he was Dong's great enemy. In the final straight, the two men took big strides and sprinted towards the finish line. Dong Shuzhao was well-trained and was still able to beat Li Yanxiang by four meters. However, being forced by Li all the way, he opened the throttle to the maximum, and as a result, he was able to break Wang Mingshen's national record of 2 minutes 6.8 seconds with an excellent result of 2 minutes 5.2 seconds, which greatly enhanced the color of men's track and field. Although Li Yanxiang was second, his result was also within 2 minutes 7 seconds, which is also commendable. Dong Jiaxie and Hou Dechong came in third and fourth.

Chen Jiayou Strives in the High Hurdles. Cao Yu gave up the high hurdles final due to the ten-event competition, so only five runners started. Chen Ling started the fastest, and Chen Jiayou was the slowest. By the fourth hurdle, the two Chens cleared the hurdle at the same time. From the sixth hurdle onwards, Chen Ling gradually fell behind. When they reached the finish line, Jiayou won by five or six meters, which was unexpected. Chen Ling finished second, Xiao Dinghua finished third, and Tao Yingjie finished fourth. Wang Huipu was fifth. Unexpectedly, according to the referee's report, Chen Ling and Wang Huipu were both disqualified for knocking down three hurdles. Xiao Dinghua and Tao Yingjie each moved up one place without effort.

Jinguang Regains the Championship in the 200m. Chen Jiayou abandoned the final because he had not recovered his energy after the high hurdles. Therefore, only seven runners started. Cheng Jinguang, learning from his failure in the 100m, dared not relax in the 200m, hoping to make up for it. The others were also scheming to occupy a position. At the start, there were two false starts due to violations, which shows the tension at the time. As a result of the competition, Cheng Jinguang actually got his wish and regained the championship, restoring his position in sprinting. Su Xiaoru was second, and Xue Jianqiu and Dong Yinchu took third and fourth place. Veteran Huang Feilong finished fifth and was out of the running.

Pole Vault Champion Fu Baolu

(Photo by Qichang)

Wang Zhenglin's Performance Improves in the 10,000m. Before the start of the 10,000m race, it was known that the championship would go to Wang Zhenglin. It was as easy as turning his hand to win the championship. Xu Yanbo is physically fit and is a good long-distance runner, but his foot movements are too slow and slightly bouncy, which puts him at a disadvantage. Zhang Quanzhou is too heavy, and it is difficult for him to improve in long-distance running. It is better to switch to other events.

Tao Yingjie Loses Form in the Hurdles. Tao Yingjie could not be optimistic in the hurdles final. This newspaper had already revealed this yesterday, and the result was as expected. Cheng Jinguang took his place, but the result still could not break the 60-second mark, which was not satisfactory. Chen Ling gave up the final for the pole vault. Otherwise, the second-place position would be difficult to say who it belonged to.

Veterans Eliminated in the 400m. The 400m race is one of the most difficult events in track and field. It requires both speed and endurance, so 400m athletes often cannot last long. Guan Changfa, He Debao, and Zhu Ruihong were all known as Shanghai's 400m experts, but unexpectedly, they were all eliminated in yesterday's final, and their positions were taken by new athletes. This shows the abundance of talent. However, I have one suggestion for all the athletes: after the third turn, everyone should proceed in a straight line and should not compete to run in the inner lane to block others. The top three had this problem yesterday and should pay more attention to it in the future. The champion, Zeng Rongzhong, achieved 53.6 seconds, which is not very common.

In the Women's 50m, Ms. Chen Shu, who won first place, is from Xiamen and is lively and loves sports. She has shown her talent in the past two National Games and middle school games. Judging by her physique, she is actually better than Qian Hangsu. However, because she has practiced sports for fewer years, her results are not as outstanding as Qian Hangsu. Li Baohui, who won second place, has developed bad habits in her running posture, which may be difficult to improve in a short time, and it will be difficult for her to achieve better results in the future.

Qian Hangsu Takes the Lead in the Women's 100m. When the women's 100m was about to begin, the sky deliberately made things difficult by increasing the southerly wind, so the results of the competition were not as good as the preliminary rounds the day before. After the gun fired, only Miss Qian Hangsu was seen taking the lead, making the people behind her gradually drift away. When she broke the white line, she was three meters ahead of the second person. Shuqing, Li Yinan, and Li Baohui competed for the second, third, and fourth positions.

Qian Hangsu Wins a Second Victory in the Low Hurdles. Only five athletes participated in the final. Qian Hangsu's victory was expected by everyone. However, due to the headwinds, the results were worse than in the preliminary rounds the day before. Zeng Huiqiong, who finished second, is also a promising talent. If she can continue to train, she will not be inferior to Qian Hangsu in the future. Xiao Jieying, who finished third, and Zhiming, who finished fourth, were at a disadvantage because of their short legs.

Qian Hangsu Overcomes Three Obstacles in the 200m. Six people started running. Watching from the judges' stand at the finish line, it was possible to distinguish each person even though they were 200 meters away, because each person had a special posture. Qian Hangsu was petite and had a fast pace, while Li Yinan was heavy and had a big stride. All the way, except for Qian, who was in the front, the other five people competed fiercely. As a result, Li Yinan won second place, and Zeng Huiqiong and Wang Huachang won third and fourth place. The result was 29.7 seconds, which was not very satisfactory. However, after kneeling down, Qian Hangsu shouted ("My mother!"), because Miss Qian participated in as many as four events. Humans are not made of iron, so how could they not be tired, especially since she is a woman from Fujian?

Qian Hangsu Breaks the National Record in the Women's Long Jump Again

Chen Rongming Sets a New National Record in the Softball Throw

Fu Baolu Carelessly Loses Jingzhou in the Pole Vault

Other Results are Close to National Records

Yesterday was the last day of the track and field competition. There were a total of seven men's and women's field events. In the women's long jump, the first and second place winners both broke the national record. The champion, Qian Hangsu, jumped 4.88 meters, and the runner-up, Chen Shuqing, jumped 4.80 meters. Chen Rongming also set a new national record in the softball throw with 42.97 meters, which is famous throughout the country. Fu Baolu, who recently unofficially set a national pole vault record of 3.84 meters, failed to officially set a new record yesterday and won the championship with 3.44 meters, which was disappointing. In the subsequent exhibition match, he reached 3.78 meters, barely meeting expectations. Miss Ma Ji won first place in the women's discus with 25.16 meters, which is commendable. It is a pity that there were no official records for comparison before. Other results, such as Hao Chunde's javelin throw of 46.16 meters, Chen Baoqiu's shot put of 12.13 meters, and Pan Chengbin's triple jump of 13.09 meters, were only slightly different from the national records, which is also commendable. The decisive battle is recorded separately as follows:

Shot Put

In the men's shot put final, the participants were Chen Baoqiu and six others. During the first week of trial throws, Gong Wanyu took the lead, followed by Chen Baoqiu and Bao Jialiang. The results were all around 11 meters, without anything particularly special. By the second week of trial throws, Gong Wanyu was still in the lead, but there was no improvement in the scores of the other competitors. In the third week of trial throws, Gong Wanyu gritted his teeth and made a powerful throw, exceeding the original record by half a meter. However, Chen Tieniu, not wanting to be outdone, roared and threw the ball to the same distance as Gong. At this point, Gong's score was 11.75 meters, and Chen's score was 11.74 meters. Having entered the final week, Gong and Chen initially did not achieve anything significant. In the fifth throw, Gong achieved 11.82 meters, while Chen at this time achieved 11.13 meters. The distance from the national record was only 0.11 meters, but catching up seemed as difficult as ascending the Shu Road. Gong and Chen both failed in the sixth throw and could only sigh in despair. In the competition for third and fourth places, Bao Jialiang and Liu Jingfeng competed with each other. In the final throw, Bao achieved 11.36 meters. The scores of the top four all broke the previous tournament record of 10.54 meters held by Cao Yu. The scores of the four are recorded as follows:

Javelin

There were fourteen participants in the javelin final. Most threw over 40 meters. Hao Chunde was a surprising standout, achieving 46.16 meters in his third throw and winning the championship. Three years ago, Hao was a champion in the national athletics scene. In the previous National Games, he represented the city and won first place in both the long jump and pentathlon. In the past year or so, he had no longer participated in the city's sports events. Many knowledgeable people predicted that his performance had declined and that he did not want to participate. However, Hao's performance in the past two days has been exceptionally good. A few days ago, he won first place in the long jump with 6.62 meters, and yesterday he won first place in the javelin and third place in the 100 meters. His performance has improved significantly compared to three years ago. It can be seen that Hao's ambition has not lagged behind others. The second place, Pan Nanshun, achieved 44.64 meters, and was the champion of the previous National Games. In yesterday's competition, most people predicted that the championship would undoubtedly belong to Pan, but he was surprisingly defeated by Hao. The top three all broke the previous tournament record of 44.07 meters held by Liu Jiayu.

First Place: Hao Chunde 46.16 meters

Second Place: Pan Nanshun 44.66 meters

Third Place: Tang Xianzhou 44.64 meters

Fourth Place: Wang Jihuai 42.98 meters

Pole Vault

The highly anticipated pole vault final was held yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m. The participants included Fu Baolu from the Northeast, who is the national record holder (3.54 meters) and the champion of the previous National Games. The spectators who came to the field yesterday all wanted to witness Fu's style and grace. There were a total of eight participants. When the height was raised to 3 meters, several people were gradually eliminated. Those who cleared 3.20 meters included Fu, Cao Yu, Wang He, and Chen Ling. Chen Ling was eliminated at 3.31 meters and finished fourth. Wang He cleared 3.31 meters and finished third. The height was then raised to 3.44 meters, and Fu Baolu and Cao Yu both cleared it. When the height was raised to 3.66 meters, Cao Yu failed three times. At this point, Fu Baolu was very relaxed, believing that his personal best was much higher, so he was still wearing long pants when jumping and did not measure his running steps. As a result, he failed to clear the bar on the first two attempts. On the third attempt, he dashed forward and cleared it, and the whole field burst into applause. However, an unexpected incident occurred: the Boy Scout holding the pole accidentally knocked the crossbar down. Fu failed to clear the bar in three attempts, so the referee ruled it a failure. Subsequently, the referee allowed him to continue jumping, but the record should be officially recorded as 3.44 meters. The subsequent attempts were all considered exhibition performances. Fu then cleared 3.66 meters and then 3.78 meters, showing that Fu's strength is not weak. He should be able to set a new record in the National Games. Fu's accidental encounter yesterday must also be attributed to his personal carelessness. When trying to jump over the height of 3.66 meters, he did not pay much attention to the first two jumps. Only on the third jump did he take off his long pants. Moreover, the pole he used yesterday was also borrowed from Chen Ling, which resulted in him not being able to break the national record, which is a pity. The second place, Cao Yu's score was also 3.44 meters. The old general's prowess is rare. Chen Ling, because he was concentrating on the decathlon, did not compete with all his strength in yesterday's pole vault. The scores of the top two broke the previous tournament record of 3.38 meters held by Li Lin. The top four are recorded below:

First Place: Fu Baolu 3.44 meters (New Tournament Record)

Second Place: Cao Yu 3.44 meters (New Tournament Record)

Third Place: Wang He 3.31 meters

Fourth Place: Chen Ling

The men's triple jump final was the last event of yesterday's finals. The participants included Gu Huo, Wang Yongmin, He Zuxi, Nong Bide, Pan Yongbin and others. The women's discus is a new track and field event in various countries, and there is no official recognized record in the country. There were twelve participants in this competition yesterday. Soccer Semi-Finals: Donghua Narrowly Defeats Youyou

The result was 3-2, gaining the right to the finals. A successful header by Li Yichen at the very end.

丨Youyou's performance was brilliant and different from the past丨

Yesterday, in the final moment, Li Yichen met Xue Wenxiu's corner kick and headed it into Youyou's goal. The score changed from a 2-2 tie to a 3-2 result, giving them the right to the soccer finals of this year's city games. Tomorrow at 3 pm, they will meet Jinan at the Zhonghua Baseball Field to compete for this year's championship. The main general encountered danger. Feng Yunyou fell ill, and Guan Xun'an was absent, reducing Donghua's strength and shaking the front line. However, they were able to turn from a disadvantaged position into a draw, and ultimately win, which is said to be due to their good fortune, and it is not an exaggeration. The entire military force had a strong left side and a weak right side, and the offense and defense were unbalanced, which almost led to a disaster. The reason lies here. It was the power of three or four special talents that turned the situation around.

Donghua Formation

Mang Jiaju Li Ning Feng Nianhan

Chen Hongguang Tu Kaiyuan Wu Youliang

Wan Xianghua Chen Jiaqiu Li Yichen Zhou Guangzhong Chen Yutian (above) Xue Wenxiu (below)

Performance, good or bad, is also an honor. Speaking of Youyou, it is inevitable to feel sorry. The first half was beyond question. With the wind helping their momentum, they were aggressive. At that time, if they had shot effectively, why would they have only won a penalty kick? Even against the wind, they were able to confront each other. Their forwards advanced in an orderly manner, and their footwork was excellent. The internal personnel were all calm and impeccable. Defeat is not something to dwell on, but it was not due to a lack of effort in the battle.

Youyou Formation

Tang Yongchun Wang Shusen Shi Jinsheng

Ye Jinmian Huang Ruihua Wang Baozhang

Li Shuoyou Sun Jinshun Hu Youcheng Xi Qiaosheng Shen Baigui

Jinshun scored with a penalty kick. Donghua kicked off against the wind.

Before long, Youyou's Li Shuoyou was active on the left flank, and Sun Jinshun led the army to follow, with great momentum. Li Ning showed his infallible header, defusing many dangers. Donghua's Chen Yutian sent two crosses, which were just right, but no one responded. Tang Yongchun came out and caught them, passing safely. Youyou suddenly changed their strategy and switched to attacking from the right. Shen Baigui took the lead and was about to enter the room when Chen Hongguang, eager to save the main general, committed a penalty foul. Sun Jinshun kicked it calmly, scoring a goal in the left corner, taking the lead.

Showing amazing skills, the audience praised. Once the record was opened, the psychology of both sides changed. At that time, Youyou attacked more than defended. Several fierce shots hit the goalkeeper. Sun Jinshun suddenly sneaked into the left flank, dribbled the ball forward, and shot without scoring. The ball went to the middle, where Li Shuoyou happened to be shooting hard at the goal. The goalkeeper Fan caught it with both hands, but suddenly dropped it. The ball rolled backwards, touching the goalpost. This was probably a matter of fate, because if it had moved slightly to the right, Donghua would have lost. With this ball saved, Donghua had a chance to live. In an instant, Wan Xianghua was extremely quiet and thought of moving. He attacked again and again, surrounding Youyou. At this time, a ball suddenly fell from the air. Li Yichen did not have time to turn around, and hooked his foot back. Without anyone knowing, it fell into the goal, making the score 1-1. The remaining five minutes of the first half also ended in the audience's praise and admiration. The victory and defeat changed in the transformation. With the wind helping Donghua, five riders advanced together. Wang Shusen was a little careless, and Zhou Guangzhong turned out in front of him. With an empty goal in sight, he actually shot it obliquely. Afterwards, Youyou launched a large army. Xi Qiaosheng also encountered the same opportunity and could not use it. Then Hu Shen and others also took the opportunity to advance, but their ambitions were not achieved. The ball situation turned, and Wan Xianghua passed it to Li Yichen, then to Xue Wenxiu. Xue shot with all his might, as heavy as a thousand pounds. It hit the goalpost, shaking as if it could not support it. In the midst of Chen Jiaqiu and Shi Jinsheng's struggle, an arm touched the ball, and a penalty was declared. Li Yichen awarded the main penalty, as he wished, Donghua took the lead with 2-1. Youyou's morale did not decline, and they continued to attack. Sun Jinshun confused people's ears and eyes, suddenly moving from left to right. He kicked with his iron leg, and the score became 2-2. Three minutes later, another change occurred. Xue Wenxiu kicked a corner, and Li Yichen's head grew eyes, and he found the ball in the crowd and met it to enter the goal, resulting in a 3-2 result and gaining the right to the final. Referee Shen Huichun, linesmen Liu Chunshu and Chen Guoyi.

Baseball Game: John Defeats Jiaotong

▲Due to Darkness, Only Five Innings Played

Result: Seven to Three

The first baseball game was held at Jiaotong University yesterday afternoon at 4:30 PM. The participants were the baseball teams from John's University and Jiaotong University. Mr. Liang, a baseball expert who returned from studying in Japan, along with his brothers, served as umpires, with Chu Cheng-song and Zeng Guangbang as base umpires. The game was originally scheduled for seven innings, but it was stopped after the fifth inning due to darkness. According to the rules, even if the game is stopped after five innings, the result can be determined. Therefore, John's University won with a score of seven to three.

The skills of the two teams were comparable. John's University won because of their composure and fewer errors. The Jiaotong University team included several overseas Chinese students who had recently returned from Honolulu and were quite knowledgeable in baseball. Jiaotong University has a long history of being the champion of Jiangnan University. However, their carelessness and mistakes were frequently seen. In yesterday's game, there was no significant difference in technique; the difference lay in the number of errors made.

John's University started on the offense first. Jiaotong University's pitcher, Wen Liandong, threw four balls in a row several times, filling the bases. He Qionghua then hit a single, and three runners scored, giving John's University an initial lead of three points. When it was Jiaotong University's turn to bat, the first three batters were out in succession, making no progress. In the second inning, John's University did not score. Jiaotong University hit three consecutive singles, and Shen Guanlan and Zhang Jinrong scored two points. In the third inning, Pang Panfang and Zhang Yongxu of John's University scored two more points. Wen Liandong of Jiaotong University hit an extremely far and high ball, which was caught by John's University's center fielder. Afterward, two more batters were struck out, and Jiaotong University scored no points again. In the fourth inning, Li Xuewen of John's University and Zhang Jinrong of Jiaotong University each scored one point. In the fifth inning, Wu Zhenbang replaced Hu Hede of John's University and scored another point. Jiaotong University scored zero points. At this point, it was already dark, and the game was stopped. As a result, John's University won seven to three. ▲Scores by Innings

Jiangsu Provincial Games Conclude Successfully, Second District Wins Overall Championship

▲Track and Field Events Set Eleven New Provincial Records

丨Mrs. Zhou Fohai Presents Awards at Closing Ceremony丨

(Zhenjiang Correspondence) Yesterday was the final day of the Third Jiangsu Provincial Games. The scorching sun hid, and a golden breeze brought coolness. All events concluded successfully. In the men's division, the Second District and Fourth District each won two championships. However, because the Second District had the highest total score in track and field, it won the overall championship. In the women's division, the Second District won the track and field and volleyball championships, also winning the overall championship. A total of eleven new provincial records were set in track and field, and several were very close to the national records. Outstanding talents such as Jin Zhongkang and Zhang Jiakui will show their skills in the National Games arena. The games lasted for four days. Because those in charge were serious and diligent, and handled matters appropriately, all order was maintained in a structured and orderly manner, and all competitions proceeded smoothly without any disputes. This good phenomenon has truly never occurred in previous games.

Seventh District Wins Chinese Martial Arts Championship

Third District Wins Men's Tennis Championship

▲Yesterday's Victory over Second District with a Score of Two to One

Yesterday's tennis final was watched by a large crowd. The four singles players from the Second and Third Districts all had excellent skills. As a result of the competition, the two districts each won one singles match. The championship depended on the doubles match to be decided in the afternoon.

In the first singles match, Zhang Jizeng of the Third District faced Sun Jianqu of the Second District. Sun was the best player in the previous National Games. On that day, he was defeated by Zhang in three straight sets. Sun's skills were not bad, but his performance was unhurried and often lured Zhang to the net, while lofting high balls to the back or taking the opportunity to execute low and fast spin shots, preventing Zhang from returning the shots. Zhang's attitude was extremely calm. Sun's shots lacked control, and there were many errors. The scores of the three sets were as follows:

Third District Zhang Jizeng 6-3 6-3 6-1 Second District Sun Jianqu

In the second singles match, Dai Guangjin of the Third District faced Chen Senrong of the Second District. Chen's serves were fierce, and his smashes were sharp and fast. Dai's returns were weak and powerless, and the ball often hit the net or went out of bounds. He lost the first two sets in a row. In the third set, Dai suddenly rallied, and his net play was miraculous, winning three games in a row. After Chen won one game, Dai won another three games to end the set. Starting from the fourth set, Dai once led with game scores of 3-1 and 4-2. However, Chen frequently attacked with heavy and powerful smashes, which Dai was unable to handle, and he lost three games in a row, allowing Chen to surpass him. At this time, Chen looked calm and composed. Whenever Dai lost a point, he would swing his racket and stomp his feet, revealing impatience and anxiety. The coach beside him told him to calm down. There were three ties in the set, but Chen became more and more courageous as he fought, and his powerful kills were endless. In the end, he won with a score of 10-8.

Second District Chen Senrong 6-3 6-4 1-6 10-8 Third District Dai Guangjin

Since the singles matches were tied, the doubles match was held at 1:00 PM to determine who would win the championship. The players on both sides remained the same. Zhang Jizeng and Dai Guangjin of the Third District had excellent cooperation. Dai played at the net while Zhang guarded the back, with few errors. Sun Jianqu of the Second District made many wild shots, and Chen Senrong, who was known for his serves, often had double faults, committing frequent suicide. In the first set, Zhang and Dai completed five games in one go. After Sun and Chen barely managed to win one game, the Third District won the first set with a score of 6-1. In the second set, the Second District once led with a score of 2-1, but it was only a flash in the pan, and the Third District won several games in a row to win the second set with a score of 6-4. In the final set, Sun and Chen tried their best to attack, but Zhang's returns were like a machine, often returning balls that were difficult to save over the net, making them impeccable. In the final game, Dai made two overhead smashes. Amid enthusiastic applause, they won the championship with a score of three straight sets.

Third District Zhang Jizeng and Dai Guangjin 6-1 6-4 6-3 Third District Sun Jianqu and Chen Senrong

Seventh District Wins Men's Basketball Championship

▲Fourth District Suffers a Miserable Defeat with a Score of 14-21

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the Seventh and Fourth Districts had a final showdown in basketball. The referee was Mr. Lu Zhongen, a famous basketball player who had attended the Far Eastern Games. After the center jump, Chen He of the Seventh District received the ball passed from the defense, took three steps, took two steps, and shot with both hands, sending the ball into the basket. Jin and Ma, the two forwards, also scored one after another. Seeing the unfavorable situation, the Fourth District tried hard to counterattack, and Zhou Heming and Yang Yitong started to score. However, the Seventh District had the upper hand, and Chen He's long shots were successful 19 times, increasing the score significantly. The Seventh District led by seven points in the first half.

In the second half, the Fourth District was still in poor form. Although the forwards were brave, they lacked luck with the ball, and they often missed. The Seventh District continued to have smooth sailing, rising steadily, with the greatest lead reaching more than ten points. In the last five minutes, the famous player Qian Dingshen was troubled. He broke through the siege and scored several times in a row, bringing the score closer. However, time was not on their side, and they suffered a miserable defeat with a difference of five points.

Overall, the Seventh District was known for its average talent and fast teamwork. The Fourth District's individual techniques had reached a good level, but their cooperation seemed to be slightly lacking. Yu Jinxiang's shooting was inaccurate, and Qian Dingshen seemed to be playing with an illness in the first half. Chen Hefang's long shots and close receptions were seamless. Jin Youde was tall and lively, truly a good player. Overall, the skills of the two teams were comparable, and the victory depended on fate rather than a lack of skill.

Discussion Committee on Teaching Subjects for Normal Schools (1)

(Nanjing, 22nd dispatch) The Normal School Teaching Subject Discussion Committee resolved this afternoon: (1) The total weekly teaching hours for normal schools, including self-study, morning exercises, extracurricular activities, etc., should be set at sixty hours; (2) The name "Rural Normal School" should be abolished, and all should be named "Normal School." Two separate tables should be established for teaching subjects: the first table is applicable to general normal schools, and the second table is applicable to normal schools located in rural areas. The first table is divided into four categories: general subjects, education subjects, education practice, and elective subjects; the second table is divided into four categories: general subjects, rural and agricultural subjects, education subjects, and education practice; (3) Simple Normal Schools should also be divided into two tables: the first table is applicable to general simple normal schools, and the second table is applicable to simple normal schools located in rural areas. The first table is divided into three categories: general subjects, education subjects, and education practice; the second table is divided into four categories: general subjects, rural and agricultural subjects, education subjects, and education practice; (4) Kindergarten Normal School subjects, education courses, should be divided into three categories: general subjects, education subjects, and education practice. It was also resolved that the percentage of hours for each category of education subject in normal schools, simple normal schools, and kindergarten normal school courses should be re-revised when determining the various teaching subjects in other normal school courses and simple normal school courses; (6) It was resolved to divide into four groups for group discussions on the morning of the 23rd, followed by a review meeting in the afternoon. The first group will work on the first table for normal schools and simple normal schools; the second group will work on the third table for normal schools and simple normal schools; the second group will work on the kindergarten normal school courses; the fourth group will work on the special normal school courses and simple normal school courses. The members of each group were identified based on those present at the meeting. Zheng Xiaocang will convene the first group, Jin Haiguan will convene the second group, Hu Shuyi will convene the third group, and Gu Shusen will convene the fourth group.

In order to ensure that normal schools have appropriate curriculum standards, the Ministry of Education, in addition to convening a curriculum standard meeting again at a later date, first discussed the teaching subjects. A discussion meeting on teaching subjects for normal schools was held at 9:00 a.m. on the 22nd in the Ministry of Education conference room. In addition to the invited committee members, the Ministry of Education also sent personnel to participate in the meeting. The meeting details are as follows:

▲ Ministry of Education Staff: The Ministry of Education staff participating in the meeting included Gu Shusen, Director of the General Education Department (in charge of this meeting), Section Chiefs Dai Yingguan and Wu Yan'yin, Clerks Weng Zhida and Xue Tianhan, Specialists Li Ximou and Guo Youshou, Li Jiaxiang, Chen Shizhen (Counselor), Dai Xiatang, Xi Fen, and Zhong Daozan (Inspectors), and Peng Baichuan, Section Chief of the Social Education Department.

▲ Committee Members Present: Of the 19 committee members invited by the Ministry of Education, the following 18 attended: Huang Jianzhong, Jin Haiguan, Huang Zhifu, Qian Yonghe, Tang Changyan, Chen Jianhan, Zhuang Zexuan, Hu Shuyi, Jiang Wenqiao, Li Qingsong, Shi Renfu, Meng Xiancheng (also representing Wang Diancun), Wu Xiaocang, Cao Chu, Zhao Shuting, Xu Benzhen, and Sun Dezhong. Only Yu Ziyi was absent due to personal matters.

▲ Outline of Proposals: In addition to the four general categories of proposed matters previously reported, including the establishment of various teaching subjects and the distribution of weekly hours for various types of normal schools and normal school courses, a proposal outline for temporary motions was added today. The draft of the various teaching subjects and total hours for various types of normal schools and normal school courses is roughly as follows: (First (Normal School) Women's Normal School) Teaching Subjects: (1) Basic Subjects (Civics, National Language, History, Geography, Arithmetic, Physics, Chemistry, Biology, Physical Education, Hygiene, Military Training (Military Nursing), Labor, Art, Music, Ethics, Home Economics); the number of teaching hours for each subject should account for several tens of percent, and the weekly average should be set at several tens of hours; (2) Education Subjects (Introduction to Education, Educational Psychology, Educational Testing and Statistics, Elementary School Teaching Materials and Methods, Elementary School Administration); the number of teaching hours for each subject should account for several tens of percent; (3) Practice hours should account for several tens of percent. The Beauty of Fashion by Su Feng

No modern woman dislikes fashion. However, generally speaking, under the (presumed) circumstances, what we see as so-called fashion is often very poor. Not only is it lacking in aesthetics, but the materials and color schemes are also flawed.

Because of the general mindset, people only seek (1) high prices; (2) imported products. They pay no attention to other essential conditions such as (1) how to coordinate colors, (2) how to tailor... and so on. Thus, fashion as fashion is merely a display of wealth and does not represent a love of beauty!

I believe that the beauty of fashion is not determined by economic conditions. Therefore, those who create fashion should never choose based on (whether the price is high).

As for (Chinese people using Chinese goods,) this is an inevitable principle, and the use of domestic silk and satin for fashion goes without saying.

(2) Autumn-style Fabric Patterns (5)

The Best Materials for Preparing Winter Clothes

By Fu

| Zhanghua's Domestic Woolen Fabric |

The autumn wind suddenly rises, scattering the backbone that has surrounded us for months, and we return to a cool realm. In such a refreshing environment, we suddenly think of the cold and harsh winter that will arrive soon, and we cannot help but shudder before it even begins. We remember the ancient saying "prepare for rain" and learn from the warning of "digging a well when thirsty." We should take advantage of this mild season to prepare some winter clothes. As soon as we talk about making winter clothes, we inevitably think of the need for woolen fabrics, because woolen fabrics are truly the best material for winter clothes. They are soft, warm, close-fitting, and can keep out the cold. They have the warmth of cotton, but cotton does not have their timeliness and beauty. However, what makes people hesitate and ponder is that people seem to think that (woolen fabrics) are imported foreign goods, and they believe that even if there are so-called domestic goods on the market, they are unreliable and incomplete. This kind of thinking is naturally unavoidable. Because we know that weaving woolen fabrics is China's newest industry. In the past, we did not know that wool could be woven into clothing. Since Europe shipped in woolen fabrics, Chinese people have competed to buy them, and the demand has surged, so some merchants have come to operate this industry. However, weaving woolen fabrics is not a simple matter. The process of weaving woolen fabrics is truly very troublesome. First, we must remove the impurities from the important raw material, wool. Then, it must be washed, combed, analyzed, and so on before it can be loaded onto a weaving machine. After that, it must go through the work of repairing, finishing, dyeing, and flattening before the woolen fabric can be made. The various machines required for such complex work cannot naturally be purchased by small operators. Therefore, for the sake of convenience, those woolen fabric merchants simply wholesale ready-made woolen fabrics from foreign countries, change their appearance, and advertise them as (domestic goods). Some of the more honest ones also wholesale woolen fabrics from foreign countries and go through their own dyeing and coloring procedures, and then they are considered (domestic goods). The better ones at least purchase their raw materials from countries such as England, Germany, and Belgium. Therefore, it is no wonder that Chinese people suspect that the woolen fabrics on the market are all (unreliable) (incomplete) domestic goods or even (foreign goods).

However, this suspicion was finally broken by the facts contributed by the Zhanghua Domestic Woolen Fabric Factory, which was established in 1929 and is now developing.

The Zhanghua Domestic Woolen Fabric Factory, with its substantial capital of one million, hired hundreds of skilled male and female workers and equipped itself with all the machines needed for the woolen fabric weaving process. Not only does it not rely on foreigners for dyeing and coloring, but also washing and weaving are done by the factory itself. Not only does it wash and repair itself, but also its wool raw materials are mostly obtained from areas such as western Zhejiang and Shandong, such as Huzhou and Caozhou. In this way, the products of the Zhanghua Factory, which weaves, spins, and dyes itself, can be said to be (reliable) (thorough) and completely authentic domestic goods, right? Who says that (domestic) woolen fabrics in the domestic market are (unreliable)? However, what are the products of the Zhanghua Factory like? According to tests by the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, they said that (firmness and durability) and elasticity are superior to imported products. As for the detailed situation, you can see the samples displayed at the factory's retail store on Nanjing Road, so I don't need to go on about it.

In short, in this (Domestic Goods Year), when the domestic economy is declining and industries are sluggish, the national people should encourage and support a factory that is striving to operate domestic goods.

(2) Autumn-style Fabric Patterns (6)

Changes in Silk Fabric Patterns

▲ Advancing with the Times by Ms. Chuan Mei

The patterns of silk fabrics in our country have historically changed very little. Luxurious items are mainly based on dragons and phoenixes, supplemented by qilin and cranes; elegant items are mostly based on plum blossoms, orchids, bamboo, and chrysanthemums, supplemented by return patterns and auspicious characters. Although their positions and sizes may have slight changes, and their colors and designs may have slight differences, their overall structure does not deviate from the above-mentioned principles, remaining the same for decades. The silk and satin left by grandmothers can still be worn by granddaughters without being criticized for being out of date. Large families often wrap silk and satin around spools and store them in chests, just like storing gold and silver jewelry. Towards the end of the Qing Dynasty, European styles gradually spread eastward, and foreign silk and satin were imported from time to time. As a result, the patterns of silk fabrics were influenced and began to change. However, the change was still slow, and its scope was not wide. In four or five years, only one or two different phenomena were slightly presented. Only those who study them very carefully can distinguish them. Until the founding of the Republic of China, imported goods increased day by day, and our country's electric silk weaving factories rose in response. As a result, the patterns of silk fabrics changed again. Sometimes it was flowers, sometimes it was birds and animals, sometimes it was people. The changes were many, and the replacements were rapid. In one or two years, they became outdated. In the past four or five years, printed silk and satin have become popular, and the process of change is even faster. After three-dimensional patterns were imported from Europe and the United States, they were immediately utilized and became popular in our country's silk fabrics. Last autumn and this spring, diagonal stripes were fashionable. Whether printed or woven, diagonal stripes were the most fashionable, sweeping the country for a time. Modern ladies all wore a piece of clothing made of it. In dance halls, movie theaters, and even on the streets, they could be seen everywhere. It was truly a grand sight for a while! But since the beginning of summer this year, this trend has declined again, and straight stripes and checks have risen in popularity. Willow crepe and willow georgette, checkered crepe, and checkered georgette all sell well. This autumn, the wind is refreshing, and new styles are rising in popularity. Recently, the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory and Sincere Company jointly held a fashion show and a large exhibition of silk crepe, with a dazzling array of beautiful products. More than a hundred kinds of new circle patterns for the twenty-second autumn style were seen, including large circles, linked circles, double-locked circles, full-ground circles, clear-ground circles, virtual-dot circles, horizontal-line circles, etc., all with unique designs and novel structures. Made into modern new dresses, suitable for both plump and slim figures, they were refreshing to the eye. More than 70,000 feet were sold at the event. Judging from this situation, it can be said to represent the standard of this season's patterns. It is said that the circle patterns were obtained by the factory after offering a generous reward for submissions, selected from more than 3,000 entries by famous artists Liu Haisu and Jiang Xiaozhao. Their vision is indeed superior, with patterns that truly represent the times. Studying the patterns of silk fabrics in the world, Paris, France, is the authority. Every spring and autumn, new styles are released, and major silk and fashion companies hold grand exhibitions. Silk merchants from all over the world send representatives to inspect everything and bring them back to their countries as the standard of the times. Noble ladies all regard them as the norm and wear them uniformly, considering it an honor. However, our country lags behind in everything. Even with regard to this pattern, we cannot be included internationally, which is truly shameful. Although it is due to the fact that our country's women's clothing is different from that of Western countries and cannot be generalized, at least in the spring and autumn of each year, our country must also have new patterns released to represent the standard of the times, so that modern ladies have a basis for reference, and then the clothing industry can make progress from time to time, showing the art of the East and avoiding falling behind others. I believe that pioneers in the silk industry, such as the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, should raise funds to hire artists to conduct research at any time and release new patterns in the spring and autumn of each year to represent the standard of an era, in order to promote the progress of silk and give our declining silk industry a glimmer of hope! Diagram of the twenty-second autumn style female overcoat woolen fabric weaving

The quality and color of clothes are a matter worth discussing. Today, in this period of national crisis when everyone is rejecting imported goods and vigorously promoting domestic products, domestic goods are indeed much more vigorous than before. However, the tailoring and style of clothing cannot be ignored. The current popular fashion is only adopting and imitating the style; it is not necessary to use foreign materials to make it. The factory has been carefully studying women's clothing recently. The New Look of Ancient Garments - Fan Yanqiao

Among the attire of ancient women, there are styles that are still applicable today. What differs is merely the length, width, and fit. Examples include:

▲ **Gui** (also known as "Zhu Yu").) *Biography of the Empresses*: "Clothing made entirely of green Zhu Yu." Commentary: "That is, the Da Ye garment, similar to the Gui garment of today." In modern terms, it is like an outer jacket worn on top. Back then, red edges were also used, suggesting a delicate and beautiful look. Also, *Inner Biography of Emperor Wu of Han*: "The Queen Mother's female attendants wore Gui made of blue silk, their eyes sparkling and their appearance pure and radiant." So, garments made of silk differed somewhat from today's versions, which are often made of wool or flannel. One emphasizes its flowing elegance, while the other prioritizes temperature regulation. However, a newly popular style of small silk shawls emerging in late summer and early autumn bears some resemblance to it.

▲ **Yu** Also seen in *Inner Biography of Emperor Wu of Han*: "The Queen Mother sat facing east in the hall, wearing a golden Da, its patterns bright, its radiance refined and serene." *Shi Ming* says: "Connected. The upper and lower parts of the clothing are connected." In modern terms, this is Western attire. Young women wear it a lot in the summer. Newlyweds especially like this style of clothing. However, it is not as luxurious as the Queen Mother's.

▲ **Daodun** *Fang Yan* states: "Large trousers are called Daodun." Also, *Biography of Zhu Bo*: "Former subordinates of the meritorious Cao Guan wore Da Zhao in winter." Commentary: "A large skirt and trousers." In modern terms, this refers to the large, bright, and vibrant trousers that can be seen underneath a woman's cheongsam. However, in the past, when women wore skirts, the size of the trousers was not noticed. Presumably, the terms "Daodun" and "Da Zhao" referred to men's clothing.

▲ **Reversed Clothing** Nowadays, women like to wear fur jackets inside out, but this is not an ancient style. *Biography of Kuang Heng in the Book of Han*: "To be rich and noble but not praised by scholars is like having a fox fur coat and wearing it inside out." Wearing clothing inside out is not honorable. Also, *Xin Xu* states: "Marquis Wen of Wei went on an excursion and saw a firewood carrier wearing a fur coat. He asked him. The reply was: 'I love the fur.' Marquis Wen said: 'If you don't know how to wrap it well, the fur will have nothing to rely on.'" This also opposes wearing clothing inside out. In the late Qing dynasty, high officials would wear fur coats inside out to show their high rank and the splendor of their clothing. Western women also have this intention. Chinese women imitate them, but in reality, they have lost the original purpose of keeping warm.

*Shen Bao* Radio Weekly

Practical Resistance and Capacitance Slide Rule

— Ming Xiang

When we are testing and designing electrical machinery, we often encounter the problem of calculating the total value of multiple resistors in parallel or multiple capacitors in series. The usual method of calculation is nothing more than using the following formula: Although the solution of this formula is not very complicated, it also takes up a lot of valuable time. Those who are not familiar with algebra will find it particularly difficult. However, by using the slide rule in this article, there is no need to use formulas, and there is no need for troublesome solutions. A very simple addition can quickly and accurately solve it.

The ruler is divided into two grids, A and B. The A number is a decimal less than one, and the B number is an integer greater than one. The A number is read from right to left, and the B number is read from left to right. The range of calculation of this ruler can be unlimited. For the sake of clarity, only ooi

丨丨Ｉooo o is noted. The method of reasoning is clear at a glance to the reader. For example, if the A number is pushed to oooi, the B number should be iooooo

When calculating, you must pay attention to whether the units of each number are the same. If they are different, they must be converted to the same unit before calculation. Now let's try a few examples to illustrate the calculation method of this ruler:

Example 1: Three capacitors are connected in series, and their capacitances are .oo3, .oo4, , oo5mf, find the total capacitance.

First find the .oo3 in the third row of A number. The corresponding value of B number in the third row of B number is 333. The B number of 004 is considered to be 250, and .005 is 200 (if the A number is in the second row, the corresponding value of the B number should also be taken in the second row. The rest are the same), the sum of each corresponding value is 333+250+200=783, and then find the B number 783, the corresponding value of its A number is .oo128, which is the answer.

Example 2: Four resistors are connected in parallel, and their resistances are 500, 650, 800, 1000 ohms. Find the total resistance. The corresponding value of A number obtained from these four numbers on the ruler is .002, .00154, .00125, .001, the sum of these four corresponding values is .00579, and then check A number 00579, the corresponding value of B is 172, that is, the total resistance is 17z ohms.

From the above examples, the calculation steps can be divided into three, first distinguish whether each calculated object is an A number or a B number, such as A number, find the corresponding value of B number on the ruler, and vice versa, then add the corresponding values together, and then find the corresponding value of the sum on the ruler, which is the final answer.

For this type of slide rule, readers who have not used it before may feel a little difficult when using it for the first time, but after a few trials, they will find it very convenient, which can really save us a lot of mental time.

Adjustment Method and Steps of Shortwave Transmitter (Continued)

— Luo Jingyu

Now we begin to discuss the adjustment steps of the regenerative oscillator transmitter.

(1) First remove the plate voltage of each stage, and set all plate-grid capacitances to zero degrees.

(2) Make the oscillator oscillate. The method is the same as described in the single oscillator transmitter, and the adjustment can be carried out in the same way. If it is a crystal type, the adjustment procedure is even simpler: because the circuit of the crystal type is generally a plate-grid resonance, and the wavelength of the crystal itself is fixed and unchanged: therefore, the drop point (that is, the standard point for the best oscillation situation) is the easiest to find.

(3) After the oscillator is adjusted, we should start the adjustment work of the amplifier stages. This step is the most troublesome and annoying in the regenerative oscillator. Because the purpose of the amplifier is to expand the original frequency, the external voltage must form an oscillating circuit in its grid circuit. And the output is definitely taken from the plate, so the plate circuit also forms an oscillating circuit. When these two oscillating circuits are calibrated to the same wavelength, that is, when its oscillating current reaches the maximum value, just like the plate-grid harmonic correction circuit, the plate current returns to the grid by means of the capacitance effect inside the vacuum tube. And this amplification stage loses its amplification purpose and oscillates. In order to remedy this defect, a kind of phase current is added to prevent the plate current from returning to the grid. The amplitude of this added reverse current must be equal to the returning current, and the phase difference between the two phases is 180 degrees. The purpose is to make the two cancel each other out, so that the plate and grid circuits can reach a state of mutual non-interference. As for the octave device after the crystal generates oscillation. Because the structure is similar to that of an amplifier, each stage must still be balanced. However, the wavelengths of its plate circuit and grid circuit are usually not calibrated to be the same. Therefore, a slightly inaccurate balance. It is also difficult to generate oscillations on its own. As for the simple principle and method of balance, the following is also described in passing. Figure 6A is the balance circuit of the Shanghai International Radio Station Fenglin Bridge transmitter. Cn in the figure is the balance capacitor. For the sake of structural simplicity, its balance coil is half of the oscillating coil. Regarding the theory of the balance circuit, it is easy to understand if we explain it with Figure 6B. In the figure, Cn = Cgp, Ln=lp. If there is a current returning from G through Cgp at this time, then Cn also has a reverse current applied to the grid at the same time, so that the opposing forces on both sides cancel each other out. (To be continued)

Small Experiences

Winding Steel Wire and Brass Wire into Springs

— Shu Dian

First burn the steel wire red to make it cool by itself, and its properties will soften. Then wind it into a spiral shape, then burn it red, and immediately throw it into cool water, and its elasticity will recover by itself. If it is brass wire, its properties are just the opposite. Immediately throw it into cold water after burning it red, and it will soften. After burning it red again, wait for it to cool by itself, and its elasticity will recover.

Ground Wire Material - Scale Rod

The ground wire needs to be buried in a low and humid place for good effect. However, most common metals have chemical reactions with water, and will corrode after a long time. Now I will tell readers to try a ground wire material with excellent effect and durability.

Take the dry battery after it is used up, take out the carbon rod in the center, and use it as a ground wire. It is not limited to one, the more the better. The place to be buried is also not limited to one place. The lead-in wire is clamped tightly on the screw at the end of the rod. It is best to bury each strip separately, and connect the lead-in wires together and use one wire to lead to the place where it is used.

This ground wire does not corrode and is not easy to dry out. Because sulfurous carbon can absorb moisture to make the vicinity moist. Moreover, it is waste utilization, which can be said to be an economical and durable ground wire.

A Message to Men

— Ms. Yin Xian

Recently, this publication had an article by Mr. Shen Yan, "A Message to Women." The words were earnest and touching. This article is written in response.

Men! You are the darlings of thousands of years! Your freedom, your authority, needless to say: among the sisterhood, you have priority in everything. Let's just talk about your spouses, are they not slaves raised by you? Whipping, insulting, abandoning, is there anything that is not carried out according to your wishes? In these times, you are envious of the superficial aspects of European and American customs, and sometimes help women by holding their coats and carrying their things. This is originally your way of showing off. How much real benefit is there for women? And you think that women are gaining face, and you are deeply afraid that if this continues, (one day men will be reversed and shout the slogan of equality). How petty and worried is this!

Let's talk about women's professions. Although it is said that small positions in agencies, schools, companies, etc. can allow one or two women to insert their feet, you think that it has a (struggle for life) with you. China is so big, production is so backward, foreign capitalism is so developed in the country, and domestic warlords are so rampant. Why don't you, as upright men, develop undeveloped industries, exclude foreign capitalists, and overthrow corrupt warlords and bureaucrats? Instead of starting from these big things, you are arguing with women about jobs, thinking that women have taken your positions, thinking that (this makes people who raise three or four boys at home complain all day long). How short-sighted, timid, and unenterprising is this?

As for the mutual jealousy and exclusion among women, it is indeed a weakness of women themselves. However, is it not the male society that creates the environment and terror that uses this weakness to make women perform tragic scenes? Vain and self-degrading women associate with married men, intending to steal the love of others. If the man who is being stolen is a perfect gentleman, how can he easily give his love to such a frivolous and weak-willed woman? Moreover, since the revolution, there have been countless events of men abandoning the old and welcoming the new, deceiving and insulting their wives, from revolutionary leaders, party and state dignitaries, to merchants and students. This situation has become a trend. If you want to remedy it, on the women's side, they should realize that they should not covet material enjoyment and harm the same sex. On the men's side, they should also act with conscience and have some humanitarian concepts, so that they can achieve the coexistence and co-prosperity of both sexes!

*Three Character Classic*

— Yan Qiao

The *Three Character Classic* is said to be written by Wang Bohou, a Confucian scholar of the Song Dynasty. People in the Ming and Qing Dynasties have made additions and revisions. Now Mr. Zhang Yantai has re-revised it and published it by the Suzhou Guoxue Association. He said: (Today's textbooks are far inferior to the *Three Character Classic*.) From the perspective of scholars, it is certainly like cats barking and dogs jumping, how can it be compared to the *Three Character Classic*, which includes everything from names to events. However, from the perspective of educational principles and the physical and mental development of children, how can a *Three Character Classic* make children of six or seven years old memorize it? If you still use the teaching methods of the past, seeking to (suddenly understand it one day) would be too unmodern. I also recited this book in the school. At that time, I used hard work to memorize it by rote, and recited it like singing folk songs. In fact, I still knew nothing. Now I also know that the content of this book is very rich. Among the four elementary books (*San Bai Qian Shen*), it is indeed the best. It can be seen that this book still requires a certain level to be worthy of reading it. As for the *Thousand Character Classic*, it is full of allusions and more difficult to understand than the *Elementary Learning*. In my opinion, it is not advisable to use it as extracurricular reading in the year of elementary school graduation, because some people do not have the ability to enter middle school and have to find a job urgently. If they do not have the opportunity to study, reading this *Three Character Classic* will give them a little common sense and be very beneficial.

From the experience of my children, I feel that the educational efficiency from kindergarten to elementary school graduation is very significant, far beyond what the school can compare. When it comes to middle school, progress is greatly slowed down due to the large number of subjects. Therefore, if we want to improve education, we still have to study at the middle school level. Since Mr. Zhang has already thought about this, why not compile some reading materials for middle school students? Isn't it more meaningful than improving the *Three Character Classic*?

Speaking of middle school reading materials, I think of comic books that are regarded as treasures by elementary school students. When they come back from school, they always have one in their hands. However, the contents are all romances and ballads, the paintings are crude, the explanations are incomprehensible, and what is especially terrible is the remaining poison of feudal ideas, which deeply penetrates the clean and fragile little brains. The lessons learned in school all day long are completely replaced by it. It seems that the education authorities, who can pay attention to details, think that this thing is insignificant. In fact, it is better to spend a lot of money and edit some teaching materials and compete for profit with booksellers, than to compile some low-level reading materials and distribute them to the people like missionaries selling Gospels. On the one hand, we should ban bad reading materials, which is a complete training.

Nothing to Talk About

— Tai Jiu

In life, one probably often feels the boredom of having nothing to talk about. For example, in a social occasion, you meet an acquaintance, ask for their name, and then what do you say? But you can't help but say something, so you have to perfunctorily talk about the weather, saying things like (the weather is really nice today). Or, for acquaintances you barely know, you might say something like (the weather is really nice), (you've been busy lately)? It wouldn't do to ignore them, but there's nothing to talk about, so you're stuck saying stuff like (you've been busy lately). Brits and Americans always say things like "Good morning" and "How are you?" It's said to be proper etiquette, but it's awfully boring. This shows that in life, one often feels the boredom of having nothing to talk about.

Unfortunately, humans can talk, and unfortunately, lots of things happen in the world. So, there should be plenty to talk about. Why bother with empty chatter? But that's not true. Events fall into two types: big and small. Big events can be divided into two: those that affect you personally, and national affairs. Of course, personal matters like jobs and love are only discussed when the time is right. As for national affairs, Confucius set the rules (don't meddle in things outside your position) and (it's a crime for someone of low status to speak out). Who dares to defy the sage's teachings and speak freely? As for small things, like (the neighbor's house was robbed last night), that seems too trivial and might not be polite, so you just don't talk about it. For these reasons, you end up with nothing to talk about. So in life, you just end up talking about the weather and whether you've been busy.

Evening Scene

— Yi Fan

On the way home: the small steamer left the city moat and entered the wide river where the Yi River meets: The ga, ga, ... of the engine drove away a flock of thousands of ducks, struggling desperately forward. Swimming also seems to be a struggle for survival.

On the distant bank, there were four or five, four or five bare-legged, bare-chested boatmen, pulling a rope forward with half their bodies. A rope tied to the mast of a clumsy boat, but they didn't sing any boatmen's songs. Otherwise, I would have suspected that I was on the Volga River.

The river, the wide, flat river in the distance, without wind or waves, was so flat that it seemed flatter than an asphalt road, if you could drive a car on it. With a slight breeze, it looked like a cobblestone road. But I have never walked such a flat road, and there seems to be no such grand avenue in the world, right?

A little further away from the city, but still able to see the high chimneys of factories and the high layers of pagodas of ancient temples: smoke was coming out of the chimneys and there was a venting sound at the same time.

The sun was running towards the back of the green mountains, and the reflected light illuminated the entire ship and the entire Henan, perhaps the entire world. There were more than fifty, more than fifty men, women, old and young, on the bank. They were carrying bamboo baskets, lunch boxes... walking forward quickly. The golden sunset shone on their entire bodies, and they seemed to be well-nourished. They were talking and laughing, as if they were very happy. This is not the first time, and even in two days, you can see a group of them holding umbrellas, showing only dozens of legs moving.

Is it the collapse of the rural economy, or the development of urban factories?

Thousands of poor farmers rushed to the factories in the city, and as a result, they were spit out by the factories and went to the graves. They seemed to be going through such a process and embellishing an evening scene on the bank.

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Fifteen: Guests Leave, Shy, Tender Feelings Surge; Visitors Come, Old Grievances and Bad News Bring Sorrow

Ji Zhi: No, let's sit outside, the view is wider. He found a seat facing out, with a few weeping willows in front, a patch of green wheat field, interspersed with a few villages in the distance. It had been a long time since he had been to the countryside, and it was quite interesting to look at. The waiter first poured a pot of tea and put it on the table, and said with a smile: You can drink a pot first. After saying that, he poured him a cup of tea, crossed his hands, stood aside and looked at him, smiling: You are getting fatter. In the past six months, I think you are more successful. Your job is very good, right? Ji Zhi smiled and said: Job? I do hard labor just like you. I rely on my skills to make a living. But what you said about being happy is true. I don't get angry at anyone else. This job was introduced by a company commander named Zhao Ziqiang. I am very grateful to him, but I don't know which battalion or company he is in, how can I find him? The waiter smiled and said: The Company Commander Zhao you mentioned, we have a regular here, a company commander surnamed Zhao, but I don't know if it is the person you are talking about? Ji Zhi said: He has a family and lives in Haidian. He speaks with a Baofu accent. The waiter said: That's right. You order some dishes and wait for him while drinking wine. Maybe he will pass by here in a while. Ji Zhi then ordered two dishes and four ounces of wine, and slowly ate and drank. At this time, it was only 10 o'clock in the morning, and the people eating lunch had not yet come. The waiter was also very idle here. While he was serving the dishes, Ji Zhi talked to him again, and said: Does this surnamed Zhao often come to your place to eat? The waiter said: They have food in the battalion. It costs more to eat out, why would they do that? Unless they are in a good mood, they will come here to patronize once or twice. (194)

Based on the environmental speculation, the subsequent steps are still seen as bleak. As a result, this month fell by another 0.0125 yuan compared to the previous day, October fell by 0.02 yuan, November fell by 0.01 yuan, December fell by 0.0075 yuan, January fell by 0.005 yuan, and February fell by 0.01 yuan.

Business Wisdom (43)

What is (Air Mail Remittance)?

What is Air Mail Remittance? It is placing the silver note or draft into an envelope, then securing it, and mailing it via airplane to the destination. This method of remittance is called Air Mail Remittance.

Air Mail Remittance is a new type of remittance service. It is both fast and reliable, and it holds an important place in the remittance business. (Currently, air routes are not long, so some legs may still require ordinary postal service.) Its speed is sometimes comparable to telegraphic transfers, and its security is the same as other voucher remittances. It allows for verification of handwriting and stamps on the draft stub. It combines the advantages of both telegraphic transfers and voucher remittances, making it popular with the general public, especially for those who urgently need funds or fear mistakes. In today's economic downturn, it meets the needs of the masses.

The term (Air Mail Remittance) has only recently appeared frequently in newspapers and books. Five years ago, the Air Mail Remittance business did not exist in our market, and the new term (Air Mail Remittance) was rarely seen. Because Air Mail Remittance relies on airplane delivery, just as telegraphic transfers rely on telegraphs. The aviation industry has only developed recently, so the Air Mail Remittance business and term have also emerged recently.

Air Mail Remittance business started in Europe and America not long ago. It has only been four years and two months since we started this business in China. I remember when the Shanghai-Chengdu air route started on July 8th, 1929 during the establishment of airmail service by the Ministry of Transportation. I was among the first to try this Air Mail Remittance innovation due to my interest in stamp collecting. This was originally launched by the postal service. Only recently have I seen several banks following suit in Shenbao advertisements, indicating the potential for the necessary development of this business.

What is Air Mail Remittance? Many merchants are asking each other with suspicion. That is why I have given a lengthy explanation.

Commentary

A Comparison of Two Events Guanghan

The sensational May 15th Incident in Japan, which shook the world, was finally judged yesterday after several interrogations by the military court. The perpetrators, including Eihan Goto and eleven others, were sentenced to four years of penal servitude each. Comparing this Japanese event, we are reminded of another incident in China: the Assassination Squad incident, which has also been clearly judged by the court. Liu Chongwu and several others were each sentenced to seven years of penal servitude.

Let's compare these two events.

The May 15th Incident in Japan was a conspiracy by military personnel to assassinate Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi, a major upheaval that shook the world. The seriousness of the case and the gravity of the charges are self-evident, but the outcome of the trial was only a four-year sentence. Looking back at the Assassination Squad incident in China, although it was also an act of transgression in the eyes of the law, the motivation and circumstances behind the crime stemmed from patriotic fervor and was a patriotic movement. However, the final verdict was a heavy sentence of seven years of penal servitude.

One event in Japan, one event in China. Killing the head of state of a country for power and profit results in only four years of imprisonment; eliminating despicable and treacherous villains for the sake of the nation and its people results in seven years of imprisonment. What else is there to say?

It is said that after the verdict of the May 15th Incident, the Japanese Fascist Party, while outwardly strongly claiming innocence, was actually quite satisfied. Only the Proletarian Party was strongly protesting the injustice, believing that compared to labor union movements, the legal punishments received by Japanese citizens were vastly different. I say that the Japanese Proletarian Party is too ignorant of current affairs and too ungrateful. Don't they see our country? Not long ago, wasn't a traitor with heinous crimes arrested in Tianjin? The result was that several guards and officials were respectfully dispatched to escort him by motorcycle to the Japanese concession. As for the youths like Liu Chongwu, they refused to stay put and insisted on stirring up trouble in the name of patriotism, so it serves them right to taste the taste of iron bars for a few years. Even if we want to cry injustice, we have no way to start!

A Mud Figure Bin Fu

The sun was scorching, and Old Xi was running with sweat all over his face. Seeing that the lush green (Precious Bubble Cottage) was in sight, he didn't know why, but a burst of uncontrollable excitement suddenly arose in his heart, and at the same time, his face covered with sweat felt a special kind of burning heat, not caused by the weather. He slowed down his pace, trying to control that complex emotion, but obviously, the power of control could not match the surge of emotion. This was especially true the closer he got to (Precious Bubble Cottage), the more uneasy he felt, although he was now pacing like (half a step), he was finally getting closer and closer to (Precious Bubble Cottage).

(Sanitary Ice Cream 丨 Ice Cream 丨) Under a large poplar tree dozens of steps away from (Precious Bubble Cottage), a group of bare-chested people gathered, some laughing, some talking, some snoring and searching for good dreams on the grass, a fat one was working hard to shake the ice cream, and a young one was loudly calling out for buyers. At this time, Old Xi's desire for the (cold) ice cream was just like the ice cream seller's desire for (long-shirted) buyers like Old Xi. Old Xi put down the square box that he had been holding under his left arm for a long time, took off his sweat-soaked summer cloth gown, hung it on the white poplar branch, and sat down on a bench in the welcoming voice of the ice cream seller. Only then did he take a breath. The three copper coins of ice cream and the ice cream seller's welcoming enthusiasm made him forget everything. He felt refreshed and forgot everything.

He felt that everyone in the world was lovely, wasn't he? The sympathy and welcome of these bare-chested people for the unfamiliar me who had been running and getting hot was so sincere and genuine! To say that they were only for the sake of ten copper coins of business, that would be too insulting to them. He thought and thought, but when he thought about the dogs, children, nanny, and hostess inside the (Precious Bubble Cottage) opposite, this easy affirmation seemed to be negated by him again.

Thinking of this, he couldn't help but pick up the square box placed on the ground. When he opened it, a mud figure of (handsome appearance) and (smiling face) of (Wuxi Big A-Fu) appeared. This attracted the curious eyes of the bare-chested people, and many children even ran over to admire it with drooling mouths. But he was stingy and immediately put it away, sighing heavily.

乂乂乂乂乂

Although it is said that Old Xi was only thirty years old, the wrinkles of worldly affairs and wind and frost, resided on his cheeks and hid the youthful vigor. Anyone would believe that he must have spent forty years of cold and heat. Although it is said that he had left university life for a full seven years, during those seven years, his time with a job was less than a short seven months. Although it is said that he also had the perfect happiness of a wife and loving daughter, the long-term unemployment made him unable to support them, and the heavy burden of his wife and children, on the contrary, only became his pain and sorrow.

He had profound knowledge, and he also had lofty ambitions. In a certain sense, Old Xi should be called a (promising) young man, but the seeds of his bumpy fate were rooted in the so-called (knowledge) and (ambition).

When his life became more and more difficult with the passage of time, he had to torment all his sharp edges and (condescend) to (entreat) friends. Gu Chong, the owner of (Precious Bubble Cottage), a classmate of his during middle school and now serving as a section chief in a certain bureau, was the only person on whom Old Xi pinned his hopes.

Section Chief Gu cherished old friendships and agreed to find him a (suitable) position at a (suitable) time in only one meeting after Old Xi's five or six visits. This (promise) comforted Old Xi greatly. He happily went back to tell his wife, which also aroused his wife's (enthusiasm). Therefore, his wife more urgently encouraged Old Xi to visit (Precious Bubble Cottage) often, so as not to let his footsteps become estranged. His wife often tirelessly persuaded Old Xi to greet Mrs. Gu more often, and his wife often stayed up all night to mend Old Xi's long gowns or repair his suits, wanting to dress Old Xi neatly, so that he would not lose face when going to (Precious Bubble Cottage). Old Xi knew his wife's painstaking efforts, but (Precious Bubble Cottage) was still a daunting path for Old Xi after all.

The hostess, maid, child, and dog inside (Precious Bubble Cottage) were the most frightening to Old Xi. When Old Xi stepped into the door, that animal, that black-haired dog with drooping ears, would bark wildly with the sound of the doorbell, running to his side and scurrying around. The guest must be embarrassed for a long time before Mrs. Gu, who was sitting at a small table in front of the middle hall making needlework, would utter a cold shout: (It's an acquaintance, what are you barking for?)

So Old Xi was relieved and was about to offer his smile to greet and thank the hostess, but the hostess had already lowered her head and buried her face in her work, so deeply.

The five-year-old child had initially shown quite a bit of goodwill towards Old Xi. However, later he must have been instigated by that fat, pockmarked nanny, because as soon as he saw Old Xi, he would cry and shout (scared), or curse (Silly Xi). Old Xi would not be angry with the child, and would always say with a smile:

(Good boy, don't cry 丨 I'll give you something fun to play with next time!)

The child's memory was the best, especially with the (provocative) reminders of that pockmarked nanny. When Old Xi went again next time and did not bring (something fun), the child would cry (to the death), so the thrifty hostess would put down her work and pull the child over, (coldly mocking as she pointed at the mulberry and cursed the locust.)
